### [181] [AirCast-SR: A Foundation Model for Kilometer-Scale Atmospheric Super-Resolution via Latent Consistency Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26130)
*Somnath Luitel,Manmeet Singh,Joshua Durkee,Abdullah Al Fahad,Naveen Sudharsan,Prabhjot Singh,Cenlin He,Harsh Kamath,Zong-Liang Yang,Krishnagopal Halder,Sandeep Juneja,Parthasarathi Mukhopadhyay,Saptarishi Dhanuka,Amit Kumar Srivastava*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AirCast-SR与EarthMind-SR提出了一种基于人工智能的超分辨率气象预测方法，可将全球气象预报从0.25度（约28公里）分辨率提升至1公里水平分辨率，实现每小时更新、长达67小时的八种耦合地表变量同时预测。该模型采用三维U-Net结合潜空间一致性模型（LCM）扩散框架，在美国本土区域训练，以GraphCast输出为输入，以NOAA AORC为真实目标，具备近零偏差和对10–100公里尺度大气结构的良好保留能力。模型在多个季节案例中表现优异，并展示出无需微调即可跨区域（如印度、德国）零样本迁移的能力。作为开源权重的基础模型，EarthMind-SR为千米级天气预测提供了新范式，支持区域微调、模型压缩及气候服务与灾害预警等下游应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数值天气预报（NWP）在千米尺度上的运算成本过高，难以满足能源、农业和灾害管理等领域对高时空分辨率预报的需求。因此需要一种高效、可扩展的替代方案来实现精细天气预测。

Method: 采用三维U-Net架构并嵌入潜空间一致性模型（LCM）扩散框架，利用美国本土区域的补丁样本进行训练，以GraphCast的0.25度预报作为输入，以NOAA AORC数据作为真实目标，实现从粗分辨率到1公里分辨率的超分辨率重建。

Result: 模型在所有变量和预报时效下均表现出近零偏差；功率谱分析显示其有效保留了10–100公里尺度的细粒度大气结构；在三个不同季节的美国案例研究中验证性能优越；且可在未重新训练的情况下成功应用于印度和德国的独立观测数据，体现强泛化能力。

Conclusion: EarthMind-SR作为开源权重的基础模型，开创了千米级AI天气预报的新范式，具备良好的跨区域迁移能力，可支持区域微调、模型压缩及多种气候与灾害预警应用，推动高分辨率气象服务的发展。

Abstract: Operational weather prediction at kilometer scales remains computationally prohibitive for traditional numerical weather prediction (NWP) models, limiting forecast access for applications in energy, agriculture, and disaster management that require fine-grained spatiotemporal detail. Here we introduce AirCast-SR, a foundation model for atmospheric super-resolution that downscales global AI weather forecasts from 0.25 degree (~28 km) to 1 km horizontal resolution at hourly temporal resolution, producing 67-hour forecasts of eight coupled surface variables simultaneously. EarthMind-SR employs a three-dimensional U-Net conditioned within a Latent Consistency Model (LCM) diffusion framework, trained on patch-based samples over the contiguous United States (CONUS) using GraphCast forecasts as input and NOAA's Analysis of Record for Calibration (AORC) as the target. The model achieves near-zero bias across all variables and lead times, and its radial power spectral density analysis demonstrates preservation of fine-scale atmospheric structure at wavelengths of 10 km to 100 km where coarser models lose spectral power. We validate EarthMind-SR across three CONUS case studies spanning winter, summer, and spring seasons, and demonstrate zero-shot global transferability over India and Germany using independent surface station observations without any retraining or fine-tuning. As an open-weights foundation model, EarthMind-SR establishes a new paradigm for kilometer-scale AI weather prediction and provides a platform for regional fine-tuning, distillation, and downstream applications in climate services and hazard forecasting.

</details>


### [182] [SilIF: Silhouette-Augmented Isolation Forest for Unsupervised Transaction Fraud Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26135)
*Venkatakrishnan Gopalakrishnan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出SilIF，一种基于轮廓系数的Isolation Forest增强方法，通过在树结构生成的表示空间中计算轮廓得分来提升异常检测性能。在IEEE-CIS欺诈检测数据集上，SilIF（alpha=1.0）平均提升0.0080 AUC-PR，且在所有五次实验中均显著优于原始IF（p=0.046）。在合成信用卡数据集上未见改进，并分析了性能差异的条件。该方法可调、易部署，适用于真实场景中的异常检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在标签稀缺的交易欺诈检测中，传统Isolation Forest虽具可扩展性但存在性能局限；为提升其检测能力，引入轮廓系数作为结构一致性度量，以增强对异常点的识别。

Method: 提取每个样本在森林各树中的路径长度，形成指纹向量；对这些指纹进行聚类，计算轮廓得分以衡量样本与其所属簇的匹配度；将轮廓得分与原始IF得分通过超参数alpha融合，实现增强型异常评分。

Result: 在IEEE-CIS Fraud Detection数据集上，SilIF相比原始IF平均提升0.0080 AUC-PR，且在所有五次种子实验中表现更优（p=0.046）；在合成数据集上无明显提升，表明其效果依赖于数据分布特征。

Conclusion: SilIF是一种可调、易于部署的Isolation Forest增强方法，能有效提升真实场景下的异常检测性能，但其增益取决于数据特性，需结合具体任务评估。

Abstract: Unsupervised anomaly detection is widely used in transaction fraud detection where labels are scarce. Isolation Forest (IF) is among the most popular classical methods due to its scalability and ease of deployment. We propose SilIF, an augmentation of Isolation Forest that adds a silhouette-based scoring layer computed in a representation space induced by the trees of the forest. For each point, we extract a vector of per-tree path lengths, cluster these "fingerprints" into structural groups, and compute a silhouette score that measures how well the point fits its assigned group versus the nearest alternative. The silhouette signal is combined with the base IF score via a single hyperparameter alpha. On the IEEE-CIS Fraud Detection benchmark (~590K transactions, 3.5% fraud), SilIF with alpha=1.0 improves over plain Isolation Forest by +0.0080 AUC-PR on average across five seeds, with SilIF winning on all five seeds (paired t-test p=0.046). We also report results on a synthetic credit-card dataset (Sparkov) where the silhouette augmentation does not improve over plain IF, and we characterize the conditions that distinguish the two outcomes. The paper presents SilIF as a tunable, easy-to-deploy enhancement to Isolation Forest with honest reporting of when it helps and when it does not. Code at https://github.com/venkat15vk/silif-anomaly-detection.

</details>


### [183] [On the Push-Based Asynchronous Federated Learning: A Bias-Correction Aggregation Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26162)
*Jiahui Bai,Hai Dong,A. K. Qin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PushCen-ADFL 是一种高效的异步去中心化联邦学习框架，通过共享中心点表示空间实现通信、聚合与本地稳定性的闭环，利用平均保持的推送求和方法纠正聚合偏差，并通过轻量级中心点正则化缓解异构性和延迟带来的模型漂移。结合发送方去重的缓冲机制，显著降低通信开销并提升鲁棒性。在视觉数据集上的实验表明，该方法在数据异构条件下最高提升6%准确率，同时通信成本降低超80%，实现了优异的精度-通信权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有异步去中心化联邦学习（ADFL）面临频繁的点对点通信、异步更新、非独立同分布（non-IID）数据等挑战，导致通信开销大、聚合偏差严重及模型漂移问题，亟需一种高效且稳定的解决方案以适应大规模异构系统。

Result: 在多个视觉数据集上验证，PushCen-ADFL 在数据异构条件下可提升最高6%的模型准确率，同时每轮推送通信成本降低超过80%，在精度与通信效率之间取得良好平衡。

Conclusion: PushCen-ADFL 有效解决了异步去中心化联邦学习中的通信开销大、聚合偏差和模型漂移问题，具备良好的可扩展性与鲁棒性，适用于大规模、异构的分布式学习场景。

Abstract: Asynchronous decentralized federated learning (ADFL) eliminates central coordination and global synchronization, making it attractive for large-scale and heterogeneous systems. However, frequent peer-to-peer communication, asynchronous updates on directed topologies, and non-IID data jointly lead to excessive communication overhead, biased aggregation and severe model drift. We propose PushCen-ADFL, a communication-efficient ADFL framework that enables stable training under asymmetric communication and delayed client participation. PushCen-ADFL couples communication, aggregation, and local stabilization in a shared centroid representation space, forming a closed loop between compression and optimization. Clients exchange centroid-form messages, apply average-preserving push-sum mixing to correct aggregation bias, and use a lightweight centroid regularization anchored in the same centroid space to mitigate drift under heterogeneity and staleness. A bounded, sender-deduplicated buffer further improves robustness under irregular asynchronous arrivals. Experiments on vision datasets demonstrate that PushCen-ADFL improves accuracy under data heterogeneity by up to 6\% while reducing per-push communication cost by more than 80\%, achieving a favorable accuracy-communication trade-off.

### [184] [When Rule Violations Are Rare: Chimera Training for Logical Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26171)
*Alejandro Ascarate,Leo Lebrat,Rodrigo Santa Cruz,Clinton Fookes,Olivier Salvado*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在视觉概念逻辑规则约束下的异常检测，提出一种神经规则评估器，将逻辑规则编译为有向无环图，并通过特征感知的子树MLP门来学习内部逻辑操作。针对训练数据中真实违规样本稀少的问题，引入了chimera训练：在特征层面构建反事实样本，通过拼接不同样本的子树特征并继承其真值标签，生成逻辑上的反例进行监督，从而无需真实异常图像即可提供有效的训练信号。该方法在CLEVRER、OpenImages和VidOR数据集上显著提升了规则级异常检测的AUROC，尤其在组合与关系规则上表现优异，同时输出异常分数和规则级归因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际异常不仅表现为罕见输入，更常是语义约束的违反，如物体共现、动作前提条件、事件的时间或关系规律等。现有方法难以处理训练中几乎无真实违规样本的情况，且传统训练方式容易产生捷径解。因此需要一种能有效学习复杂逻辑规则并检测违反的方法。

Method: 提出神经规则评估器，将逻辑规则转化为有向无环图；每个节点使用MLP门映射子节点特征与边级否定到父表示及规则满足概率；采用基于真值标签的精确布尔传播进行中间监督；引入chimera训练机制，在特征层面拼接来自不同样本的子树特征，保持原始真值标签，通过逻辑运算生成反事实目标，以提供监督信号。

Result: 在CLEVRER、OpenImages和VidOR数据集上，该方法在规则级异常检测任务中显著优于独立事件基线和同图像语义训练基线，特别是在组合性与关系性规则上提升明显；可输出标量异常得分和规则级归因。

Conclusion: 本文提出的神经规则评估器结合chimera训练策略，能够有效应对训练中缺乏真实违规样本的问题，实现对复杂逻辑约束下异常的有效检测，具备良好的可解释性与泛化能力。

Abstract: Many practical anomalies are not merely rare inputs, but violations of semantic constraints: objects co-occur in structured ways, actions imply preconditions, and events satisfy temporal or relational regularities. We study anomaly detection in this setting, where constraints are given as logical rules over learned visual concepts, but real rule violations are rare or absent during training. We propose a neural rule evaluator that compiles each constraint into a directed acyclic graph and learns feature-aware subtree MLP gates for its internal logical operators. Each gate maps child features and edge-level negations to a parent representation and a rule-satisfaction probability, with intermediate supervision obtained from exact Boolean propagation over ground-truth concept labels. The key difficulty is that same-image training data often provide insufficient coverage of informative truth configurations and also allow shortcut solutions. To address this, we introduce chimera training: an operand-level counterfactual construction at the feature level. Instead of mixing input images, we concatenate subtree features from different samples; each operand keeps the hard truth label of the sample it came from, and the chimera target is obtained by applying the node's logical operator to those inherited labels. This supplies supervised logical counterexamples without requiring real anomalous images. Across CLEVRER, OpenImages, and VidOR, the resulting evaluator improves rule-level anomaly AUROC over independent-events and same-image semantic-training baselines, especially for compositional and relational rules. The method yields both scalar anomaly scores and rule-level attributions.

### [185] [InfoQuant: Shaping Activation Distributions for Low-Bit LLM Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26175)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后训练量化方法在处理激活分布时未能充分考虑其对低比特均匀量化器的适配性，导致即使数值平滑仍存在较大量化误差。因此需要从信息论角度重新设计激活分布以降低量化误差。

Method: 基于信息论分析，提出量化友好的激活分布应具备小范围和良好分散性；引入峰值抑制正交变换（PSOT）和自适应异常值选择机制，实现无需训练的激活重分布。

Abstract: Low-bit activation quantization remains a major bottleneck in efficient large language model (LLM) deployment. The difficulty is not only that activations contain outliers, but that their distributions are often poorly matched to a low-bit uniform quantizer. Existing post-training quantization (PTQ) methods suppress peaks, balance channels, or minimize reconstruction error, yet they rarely specify what activation distribution is actually easy to discretize. As a result, activations may appear numerically smoother while still incurring large quantization error because the quantization range remains wide or most values collapse into a few levels near the mean. We recast activation transformation as quantizer-facing distribution design and analyze quantization error from an information-theoretic perspective. Our analysis shows that quantization-friendly activations should jointly have a smaller numerical range and sufficient dispersion within that range. Guided by this analysis, we propose InfoQuant, a train-free method that employs Peak Suppression Orthogonal Transformation (PSOT) to shape activations into more quantization-friendly distributions. We further introduce adaptive outlier-token selection to improve the robustness of PSOT during optimization. Across multiple LLM families, InfoQuant consistently outperforms prior PTQ and end-to-end training baselines. Under W4A4KV4, it preserves 97% of floating-point accuracy on average and reduces the LLaMA-2 13B performance gap by 42% over the previous state of the art. Code is available at [https://github.com/LLIKKE/InfoQuant](https://github.com/LLIKKE/InfoQuant)

### [187] [Max-Window Scale Estimation for Near-Lossless HiF8 W8A8 Quantization-Aware Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26189)
*Yingying Cheng,Jinquan Shi,Li Zhou,Zhiyang He,Zhaoyi Sun,Fan Zhang,Jie Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了HiF8 W8A8量化感知训练（QAT）在OpenPangu-Embedded-1B模型中的问题，通过延迟张量缩放（DTS）视角识别出两种独立的失败模式：(i) amax饱和，导致前向传播中缩放估计延迟引发知识敏感表征被静默破坏；(ii) 灾难性遗忘，由过激学习率覆盖预训练常识知识。两者均无法通过训练损失察觉。提出基于64步历史窗口的保守max算法DTS策略解决amax饱和，结合500步BF16预热+10^{-5}学习率的QAT缓解遗忘。二者协同可实现与BF16基线相当性能（MMLU、HellaSwag、ARC-Challenge下降<0.6%），训练损失绝对百分比误差仅0.11%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低比特浮点量化感知训练（QAT）虽提升大模型部署效率，但存在隐蔽的失效模式，传统训练指标无法捕捉其影响，尤其在知识敏感任务上表现退化。亟需系统性分析并修复这些隐藏缺陷以保障模型性能。

Method: 采用延迟张量缩放（DTS）框架，设计八组受控实验，对HiF8 W8A8 QAT进行诊断；提出保守max算法处理amax饱和，结合长周期BF16 warmup与低学习率策略抑制灾难性遗忘。

Result: 最终配置实现0.43% MMLU、0.58% HellaSwag、0.22% ARC-Challenge性能下降，训练损失绝对百分比误差仅为0.11%，与匹配的BF16基线接近，验证了双策略的有效性。

Conclusion: QAT中的隐性失败模式（amax饱和与灾难性遗忘）可通过DTS框架有效识别；仅依赖训练损失不足以评估模型质量；必须结合保守缩放策略与渐进式训练机制才能实现高效且保真的低比特部署。

Abstract: Quantization-aware training (QAT) with low-bit floating-point formats enables efficient LLM deployment, yet introduces subtle failure modes invisible to standard training metrics. We present a systematic study of HiF8 W8A8 QAT for OpenPangu-Embedded-1B through the lens of Delayed Tensor Scaling (DTS). Across eight controlled experiments, we identify and disentangle two orthogonal failure modes: (i)amax saturation, where delayed scale estimates silently corrupt knowledge-sensitive representations via forward-pass clipping, and (ii)catastrophic forgetting, where an aggressive learning rate overwrites pretrained commonsense knowledge independently of quantization. Neither is detectable from training loss alone. We address amax saturation with a conservative max-algorithm DTS strategy over a 64-step history window, and mitigate forgetting via a 500-step BF16 warmup followed by QAT at lr=10^{-5}. Both fixes are necessary and sufficient: our final configuration achieves 0.43% MMLU drop, 0.58% HellaSwag drop, and 0.22% ARC-Challenge drop versus a matched BF16 baseline, with a training loss APE of only 0.11% over 10,000 steps.

Method: 将时间序列建模为时延系统的动态混合，利用马尔可夫参数序列构建系统张量，通过张量分解提取历史模型，动态选择最适配当前状态的系统模型。

Abstract: This research addresses the problem of adaptive modeling in time-series data streams with clear input-output relationships. This problem is challenging because rapid system changes (regime shifts) caused by environmental factors or input delay changes degrade model performance, and the trade-off among accuracy, robustness, and memory usage arises when using multiple small models for each time-series pattern. To address these issues, this paper presents an online framework/method that treats streaming time series as dynamic mixtures of time-delay systems. This framework maintains robustness of model tracking and reduces memory usage by summarizing past regimes using a fixed-length representation that captures both the system dynamics and input-output delays. Concretely, this approach constructs a summary system tensor using the system's Markov parameter series, capturing both dynamic behavior and delay characteristics. If necessary, a tensor decomposition algorithm extracts relevant past models from the tensor and helps select the system that best fits the current regime. This method enables rapid adaptation to environmental changes and is computationally efficient. Tests on real datasets show that DelayMix consistently outperforms other methods, achieving superior forecast accuracy and faster adaptation to delays, especially for highly non-stationary data.

We demonstrate that these structural methods individually enhance predictive accuracy, and their integration yields synergistic improvement. Crucially, by leveraging these experimental restraints, AIMS-Fold achieves higher accuracy on challenging induced proximity targets than purely computational, unguided state-of-the-art models like Boltz-2. Result: CoAD在多个高质量基准数据集上显著超越当前主流深度学习与传统数据挖掘方法，在异常检测精度、模型效率与可扩展性方面表现优异，尤其适合大规模实时应用。

Conclusion: CoAD通过融合分类与重构的优势，实现了对复杂、细微异常的有效检测，验证了深度学习在时间序列异常检测中的巨大潜力，并具备良好的实用性与部署前景。

Abstract: Time series anomaly detection (TSAD) has long been a hot research topic in data mining due to its various applications. Recent studies challenge the effectiveness of popular deep learning methods for TSAD, suggesting their failure in detecting subtle and prolonged anomalies. Outlier Exposure (OE) and Masked Autoencoder (MAE) emerge as two promising paradigms (classification and reconstruction) for solving the above problems. However, OE-based methods are constrained by poor generalization, while MAE-based methods are limited by masking misalignment issues. To address these limitations, this paper proposes a novel framework, CoAD, which unifies the two paradigms to leverage their complementary strengths while mitigating their respective weaknesses. In this framework, the classification module generates probability-informed soft masks for the reconstruction module, which in turn alleviates the generalization problem of the classification module. This cooperative design enables CoAD to effectively detect subtle and complex anomalies that are often overlooked by existing methods. Additionally, the classification module is carefully designed to resolve issues related to improper classification granularity and the neglect of frequency information. Extensive experiments on high-quality benchmark datasets, conducted under rigorous evaluation protocols, demonstrate that CoAD significantly outperforms both state-of-the-art deep learning and traditional data mining methods, highlighting the potential of deep learning in TSAD. Moreover, CoAD is lightweight and substantially faster than existing SOTA methods, demonstrating its practical value for large-scale, real-time applications.

</details>


### [191] [On the Role of Inductive Bias in Time-Series Pretraining: A Case Study in Learning Generalizable Representations for Clinical Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26194)
*Sharmita Dey,Diego Paez-Granados*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在脊髓损伤（SCI）病理步态分析中，如何通过PathoFM预训练模型设计合适的归纳偏置，以实现跨任务和跨受试者的有效迁移。提出一种基于编码器的Transformer模型，采用三种互补目标：局部补全（重建被掩码的连续片段以保持局部结构）、时间连续性（从观测前缀预测被掩码的中段以保证平滑性和因果一致性）以及无监督上下文动态（基于受试者示例窗口的注意力支持-查询重建）。实验对比了不同目标组合（分组/对比、动态驱动、生成重建），发现以动态为中心的混合目标表现最佳，兼顾分类与回归任务的性能；仅用重建目标虽能保留波形结构但分类性能较差，而分组目标虽增强判别性但损害连续变量的精度。结论表明，结合局部重建与时间连续性，并在有示例访问时加入上下文条件，可获得鲁棒的泛化表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床时间序列学习受限于小规模、异质性队列及协议漂移，下游任务涵盖分类（如病理诊断）与回归（如时间预测）。因此需要基础模型预训练，但关键问题在于应施加何种归纳偏置以确保表示在不同任务类型和受试者间有效迁移。

Method: 提出PathoFM，一种基于编码器的Transformer模型，对多变量步态窗口进行预训练，包含三个互补目标：1. 局部补全（重建被掩码的连续片段）；2. 时间连续性（从观测前缀预测中段延续）；3. 无监督上下文动态（基于受试者示例窗口的注意力机制进行支持-查询重建）。

Result: 实验表明，以动态为中心的目标混合在跨任务迁移上表现最平衡。分组类目标提升分类判别力但降低回归精度；纯重建目标保持波形结构但分类性能弱。结合局部重建与时间连续性，并在存在示例时引入上下文条件，能实现最优的受试者泛化能力。

Conclusion: 在病理步态分析中，将局部重建与时间连续性相结合，并在实际可行时引入受试者上下文条件，是构建鲁棒、通用且跨任务有效的表示的关键策略。

Abstract: Clinical time-series learning is routinely constrained by small, heterogeneous cohorts and protocol drift, while its downstream use spans both classification (e.g., pathology diagnosis) and regression (e.g., temporal forecasting). These constraints make foundation-model pretraining appealing, but raises an important question of which inductive biases should the pretraining objective impose so that representations transfer across task types and subjects. We study this question in pathological gait analysis for spinal cord injury (SCI) via PathoFM, an encoder-centric transformer pretrained on multivariate gait windows with three complementary objectives: Local Completion (reconstruct contiguous masked spans to enforce local structure), Temporal Continuity (predict a masked mid-horizon continuation from an observed prefix to enforce smoothness and causal consistency), and Unsupervised In-Context Dynamics (support-query reconstruction conditioned on subject exemplar windows via attention). Empirically comparing objective families (grouping/contrastive, dynamics-based, and generative reconstruction), we find that dynamics-centric mixtures produce the most balanced transfer: grouping objectives favor discriminative margins but can degrade magnitude fidelity needed for continuous targets, whereas reconstruction-only objectives preserve waveform structure but may underperform on classification. Overall, combining local reconstruction with temporal continuity, and adding in-context conditioning when exemplar access is realistic, yields robust subject-generalizing representations.

### [192] [The Bridge-Garden Dilemma in LLM Distillation: Why Mixing Hard and Soft Labels Works](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26246)
*Guanghui Wang,Kaiwen Lv Kacuila,Zhiyong Yang,Zitai Wang,Jin-Wen Wu,Longtao Huang,Qianqian Xu,Qingming Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于桥花园分解理论的混合知识蒸馏方法，通过自适应结合硬标签和软标签，在语言建模中显著降低暴露偏差，提升学生模型性能。该方法在多个教师-学生对（如Qwen、Llama、Gemma、DeepSeek）上优于现有基线，同时将训练成本降低9.7倍，实现高效模型压缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识蒸馏方法中，仅使用软标签虽信息丰富，但可能引入暴露偏差；而仅使用硬标签又损失多样性。本文旨在解决训练与推理分布不一致的问题，提升蒸馏效果。

Method: 提出桥花园分解理论，将生成过程分为‘桥’（需精确预测）和‘园’（可灵活预测）两类，并设计自适应混合监督策略，动态平衡硬标签与软标签的使用。

Result: 在七个教师-学生对及推理与编码任务上，所提方法优于基于发散性和在线策略的基线，且训练成本降低9.7倍。

Conclusion: 混合使用硬标签与软标签能有效缓解暴露偏差，桥花园分解为理解蒸馏机制提供了新视角，所提方法实现了高性能与高效率的统一。

Abstract: Knowledge distillation (KD) transfers knowledge from a large teacher model to a smaller student. In language modeling, the student is trained either on tokens sampled from the teacher (hard labels) or the teacher's full next-token distribution (soft labels). Despite soft labels appear strictly richer, we find that mixing hard and soft labels consistently yields better results. Crucially, we show that this gain cannot be explained by closer teacher matching during training. Instead, it comes from reduced exposure bias, the mismatch between training and inference distributions. To explain this phenomenon, we introduce the Bridge-Garden Decomposition theory, which categorizes generation steps into two types: Bridges, where the next token must be exact, and Gardens, where it can be flexible. We show that hard-only KD excels in Bridges by avoiding risky deviations, while soft-only KD preserves diversity in Gardens. A hybrid strategy handles both cases and, as a result, reduces exposure bias across the sequence. Guided by this theory, we develop a family of Bridge-Garden hybrid supervision methods that adaptively balance hard and soft labels. Across a primary suite of seven teacher-student pairs (including Qwen, Llama, Gemma, and DeepSeek) and benchmarks in reasoning and coding, our approach outperforms divergence-based and on-policy KD baselines while reducing training cost by 9.7x, enabling efficient model compression. Code is available at https://github.com/ghwang-s/bridge_garden_hybrid_kd_release.

</details>


### [193] [Quantized Keys Steal Attention: Bias Correction for KV-Cache Compression in Video Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26266)
*Tuna Tuncer,Felix Becker,Thomas Pfeil*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对视频扩散模型中KV缓存量化导致注意力偏差问题的解决方案。由于软最大函数的凸性，量化噪声会放大缓存键的贡献，引发Jensen偏差，导致当前块注意力分配受损。作者通过在运行时基于量化步长和查询范数计算的一阶修正项，有效消除该偏差。采用二阶泰勒近似，额外计算开销极小且无需额外内存。在MAGI-1、SkyReels-V2和HY-WorldPlay数据集上，使用INT2量化时，该方法几乎恢复了BF16精度下的视频质量，并优于INT4量化，同时节省50%内存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频扩散模型依赖KV缓存以避免重复计算，但随着视频长度增加，缓存成为主要内存瓶颈。虽然量化缓存可缓解内存压力，但会因量化噪声引入系统性偏差，导致视频质量下降。核心问题是量化引起的注意力权重失衡，尤其是缓存键被过度强调。因此需要一种高效且无损的量化补偿机制。

Method: 提出一种基于注意力分数的偏差校正方法，利用量化步长与查询范数在线计算修正项。通过二阶泰勒展开近似，实现低计算开销的实时校正，不增加额外内存占用。该方法可无缝集成至现有量化框架中。

Result: 在INT2量化下，所提方法在多个基准数据集上实现了接近BF16精度的视频质量；性能超越标准INT4量化，同时减少50%内存使用，验证了其高效性和有效性。

Conclusion: Jensen偏差是量化KV缓存导致视频质量下降的关键原因。通过轻量级在线校正，可在不增加内存的前提下显著提升量化视频生成质量，为长视频生成提供了高效的内存优化方案。

Abstract: Chunk-wise autoregressive video diffusion models rely on a KV cache of previously generated chunks to avoid redundant computation, but this cache quickly becomes a memory bottleneck as videos grow longer. Methods that quantize the KV cache to low bitwidths reduce memory pressure but degrade video quality. We show that a key driver of this degradation is a systematic bias in attention weights: due to the convexity of the exponential in softmax attention, quantization noise inflates the contribution of cached keys, a phenomenon we call the Jensen bias. This effect causes quantized keys to steal attention mass from the unquantized current chunk. We derive a per-attention-score correction that removes this bias in expectation, computed on the fly from the quantization step sizes of the cached keys and the query norm. Using a second-order Taylor approximation, the additional computational overhead is negligible, and no additional memory is needed alongside the cache. Evaluated on MAGI-1, SkyReels-V2, and HY-WorldPlay at INT2 quantization, our correction recovers most of the quality lost to aggressive quantization, reaching near-BF16 video quality, and can outperform INT4 quantization while using 50% less memory.

</details>


### [194] [Scaling World-Model Reinforcement Learning Through Diffusion Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26282)
*Xiaoyuan Cheng,Wenxuan Yuan,Zhancun Mu,Yuanzhao Zhang,Yiming Yang,Hai Wang,Zhuo Sun,Che Liu*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于世界模型的强化学习方法受限于模型偏差和误差累积，更关键的是存在搜索与价值学习之间的结构错位：策略改进依赖于独立于搜索的非搜索策略所诱导的价值函数，导致训练不一致和次优学习。

Method: 提出 Model-Based Diffusion Policy Optimization (MBDPO)，将策略优化重新定义为在潜空间世界模型中对搜索轨迹的扩散过程；从收集的数据集中提取隐式能量函数以锚定策略，从而在优化过程中修正得分场，实现搜索与策略学习的统一。

Result: MBDPO 在多任务离线预训练、在线学习以及离线到在线微调等多种设置中表现优异；在大规模数据集上进行离线预训练时，随着模型容量增加，性能呈现持续且单调的提升，验证了其可扩展性。

Conclusion: MBDPO 通过将搜索与策略优化统一于扩散框架，有效缓解了传统世界模型方法中的结构性错位问题，显著提升了策略学习的效率与可扩展性，为大规模模型基强化学习提供了新的可行路径。

Abstract: Model-based reinforcement learning (RL) can be effectively supported at scale through the use of world models. However, in practice, scaling such approaches remains fundamentally limited. A commonly recognized challenge is model bias and error compounding, which degrade long-horizon predictions. Beyond these issues, we identify a more critical yet underexplored bottleneck: a structural misalignment between search and value learning in existing world model approaches. In particular, policy improvement often relies on value functions induced by a separate, non-search policy, resulting in training inconsistency and ultimately suboptimal learning. To address this limitation, we propose Model-Based Diffusion Policy Optimization (MBDPO) in world models, a framework that unifies search and policy optimization through diffusion policy representations, thereby unlocking the potential of world models for scalable policy learning. Instead of constructing an explicit planner over a learned world model, we reformulate policy optimization as a diffusion process over searched trajectories in latent world models. In this view, we extract an implicit energy function from the collected dataset that anchors the policy, enabling MBDPO to refine the score field for policy optimization while mitigating misalignment. We evaluate MBDPO across a wide range of settings, including multi-task offline pretraining, online learning, and offline-to-online fine-tuning. In the offline regime, we further investigate its scaling behavior by pretraining on large-scale datasets, observing consistent and monotonic performance gains with increasing model capacity.

Abstract: This work addresses the problem of learning the dynamics of high-dimensional probability densities over time using unlabeled samples, without assuming access to trajectory information. We introduce two-parameter flows that learn only sampling-time transports from a base distribution to each marginal and then extract a physics-time velocity by regressing on coupled synthetic trajectories. We prove that the resulting physics-time dynamics are unique and inherit regularity from the sampling-time transports. Because we can build on standard, well-developed conditional flow matching techniques for learning the base-to-marginal transports, our approach scales to high dimensions and avoids per-step optimal-transport couplings, while allowing admissible non-gradient dynamics that can naturally explain rotational or circulating physics phenomena.

### [198] [QAM-W: Joint 2D Codebook Quantization for LLM Weights via Hadamard Rotation and Activation-Aware Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26339)
*Preetam Sharma,Kacper Dobek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出QAM-W，一种基于正交振幅调制的权重量化编码器，通过L2归一化、块哈达玛旋转、二维坐标配对和单个Lloyd-Max码本量化，恢复权重行间的坐标结构。在跨模型实验中，5.5比特/权值下性能接近BF16，仅需32%权重比特即可达到SmoothQuant W8A8水平；联合二维编码优于极坐标编码2-15pp PPL，且与KL散度高度相关（ρ=0.99），验证了理论边界。3.5bpw适用于容错架构，5-6bpw为质量保持关键区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标量后训练量化方法忽略权重行内的坐标结构，导致信息损失，影响量化性能。本文旨在通过引入结构化编码方式，恢复并利用权重的内在几何关系，以提升低比特量化下的模型表现。

Method: 对每行权重进行L2归一化，执行块哈达玛旋转，将成对元素映射为二维坐标，使用针对单位圆高斯分布训练的单一Lloyd-Max码本进行量化，并结合激活感知的通道级缩放。

Result: 在5.5 bpw下，所有模型的PPL与BF16相差小于±0.4%，达到SmoothQuant W8A8性能但减少32%权重比特；二维联合编码优于极坐标编码2–15 pp ΔPPL；配对KL散度与ΔPPL高度相关（Spearman ρ=0.99）；3.5 bpw表现良好，5–6 bpw为关键质量保区。

Conclusion: QAM-W通过恢复权重行内结构，在低比特量化中实现高质量压缩，尤其在5–6 bpw区间表现出显著优势，为高效大模型量化提供了新范式。

Abstract: Scalar post-training quantizers discard pairwise coordinate structure within weight rows. We introduce QAM-W (Quadrature Amplitude Modulation for Weights), a codec that recovers this structure: each row is L2-normalized, block-Hadamard rotated, paired into 2D coordinates, and quantized against a single Lloyd-Max codebook trained on the unit circular Gaussian, with activation-aware per-channel scaling. In a cross-model study spanning five LLMs from four families (1.1B--13B parameters) and eight quantized configurations, the activation-aware variant at $\approx 5.5$ bpw stays within $\pm 0.4\%$ of BF16 WikiText-2 perplexity on every model, matching the SmoothQuant W8A8 quality envelope at $32\%$ fewer weight bits. Joint 2D coding outperforms polar (amplitude $\times$ phase) coding by 2--15~pp $Δ$PPL at equal bitrate, and paired KL against BF16 tracks $Δ$PPL\% at Spearman $ρ= 0.99$ across 37 (method, model) rows, consistent with a monotone composite bound from codec distortion to KL divergence. A 3.5~bpw variant is competitive on quantization-tolerant architectures. At strict 4~bpw, the rotated-codebook frontier method QTIP outperforms QAM-W; the contribution is the quality-preserving 5--6~bpw band.

</details>


### [199] [MechRL: Reinforcement Learning Agents Perform Circuit Discovery for Mechanistic Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26343)
*Barsat Khadka*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将电路发现重构为强化学习问题，使用PPO算法在GPT-2 small的144个注意力头中进行搜索，通过零消融与对比奖励机制，在多任务环境中成功识别出诱导和IOI任务中的关键注意力头，并在未见过的文档字符串补全任务上实现96%的性能天花板，表明该方法具备可迁移性与有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机制可解释性方法需为每个新任务定制分析流程，缺乏通用性；本文旨在构建一种可迁移、自动化的电路发现框架。

Method: 将注意力头选择建模为离散动作空间的强化学习问题，采用PPO算法，结合零消融与对比奖励（减去一般预测损失的损害，保留目标任务损失的损害）来指导策略学习。

Result: 单一策略在训练任务上达到每回合最优表现，在未见任务上通过五次采样规划恢复96%的性能上限；所选注意力头与文献中公认的非冗余头高度一致，冗余类别被正确忽略。

Conclusion: 基于因果干预的强化学习是识别单头瓶颈的有效且可迁移的方法，可作为路径修补等现有方法的补充。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability has identified small sets of attention heads that implement specific behaviours in transformer language models, but recovering these circuits typically requires a bespoke analytical pipeline for each new task. We recast circuit discovery as a reinforcement-learning problem. An agent operates over the 144 attention heads of GPT-2 small as a discrete action space; each action triggers a zero-ablation and a contrastive reward that subtracts the ablation's damage to general next-token prediction from its damage to the target task. A single PPO policy, trained on two tasks (induction and IOI) in a vectorised multi-task environment, attains the per-episode oracle on both training tasks and on a held-out third task (docstring completion). Its preferred heads coincide with the canonical heads of established literature on precisely the axes those papers identify as causally non-redundant under single-head ablation; the categories they identify as redundant are correctly de-prioritised by the agent. On the held-out task, best-of-five planning recovers 96\% of the oracle ceiling with no task signal supplied at evaluation. These results indicate that reinforcement learning over causal interventions is a viable, transferable substrate for identifying the single-head bottlenecks of mechanistic circuits, complementary to existing path-patching approaches.

### [200] [When Correct Demonstrations Hurt: Rethinking the Role of Exemplars in In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26350)
*Chenghao Qiu,Chunli Peng,Yufeng Yang,Kuan-Hao Huang,Yi Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了在上下文学习（ICL）中，演示示例的正确性并不等同于其有效性，某些正确的演示反而会降低ICL准确率。作者提出任务保持扰动框架，仅改变示例输入但保持其为任务的有效实例，从而研究正确性与实用性之间的差距。实验表明，这类扰动会引发‘上下文证据偏移’，导致模型使用的上下文信息混合发生变化，进而影响性能，尤其在小模型、复杂任务和高扰动比例下更为显著。研究强调，鲁棒ICL需同时评估演示的正确性和其对上下文推理的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对上下文学习（ICL）的理解通常认为正确示例能提升性能，但本文发现即使示例正确，其实际效用也可能很低甚至有害，因此需要探究正确性与实用性之间的脱节现象。

Method: 引入任务保持扰动方法，包括标签更新型扰动（改变语义并重算目标）和严格的目标保持型扰动（保留原目标），通过改变示例输入但维持任务一致性，分析其对模型推理的影响。构建框架以量化扰动如何改变模型所依赖的上下文证据分布。

Result: 在情感分类、逻辑推理和数学应用题任务上，任务保持扰动后的演示显著降低了ICL性能，尤其对小模型、复杂任务和高扰动比例敏感。证明了正确性不等于实用性，并揭示了‘上下文证据偏移’作为失败机制的存在。

Conclusion: ICL的鲁棒性不仅取决于示例是否正确，更取决于它们如何影响模型的上下文推理过程。未来设计有效的演示应考虑其对上下文证据分布的影响，而不仅仅是输出正确性。

Abstract: In-context learning (ICL) is often motivated by the intuition that demonstrations help because they provide correct input-output examples. However, we reveal a counterintuitive phenomenon: correctness does not guarantee exemplar utility, and some correct demonstrations can even reduce ICL accuracy. To study this correctness-utility gap, we introduce task-preserving perturbations, where only the exemplar input is changed, while the example remains a correct instance of the same task. Concretely, each perturbed exemplar is assigned the target induced by the task mapping. This framework covers both label-updating perturbations, where task-relevant semantics change and targets are recomputed, and stricter target-preserving perturbations, where the original target remains valid. We formalize the resulting failure mode as contextual evidence shift: task-preserving perturbations can change the effective mixture of evidence used by the model for contextual inference, thereby separating exemplar correctness from exemplar utility. Across sentiment classification, logical reasoning, and math word problems, we find that task-preserving perturbed demonstrations can substantially degrade ICL performance, especially for smaller models, harder tasks, and higher perturbation ratios. Our results show that robust ICL requires evaluating not only whether demonstrations are correct, but also how they influence contextual inference. Code is available at https://github.com/Chenghao-Qiu/Task-Preserving-ICL.

### [201] [Energy-Gated Attention and Wavelet Positional Encoding: Complementary Inductive Biases for Transformer Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26355)
*Athanasios Zeris*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出两种新组件：能量门控注意力（EGA）和莫莱特位置编码（MoPE），以弥补标准Transformer注意力在信息能级敏感性和尺度选择性局部性上的不足。EGA通过学习的能级估计来门控值聚合，决定关注哪些令牌；MoPE使用可学习的高斯窗波浪函数替代固定正弦编码，自适应地调整位置-频率定位。实验显示，单独使用时EGA提升性能，而MoPE略低于基线；但两者结合后性能显著超越各自之和（+0.119验证损失），表现出超加性效果。该结果表明，能级敏感性和局部性是互补的归纳偏置。消融实验进一步证明，结构化的谱先验不如可学习的自由参数表现好，且互补组件之间存在协同增益。所有实验在小规模下进行（≤6M参数，字符级任务，单种子），未来需在更大规模、多种子条件下验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Transformer注意力忽视输入的信息结构，缺乏对关键令牌能级敏感性和不同频率下位置影响范围的建模能力。为提升模型对复杂输入结构的捕捉能力，需要引入新的归纳偏置。

Method: 提出能量门控注意力（EGA）与莫莱特位置编码（MoPE）。EGA通过线性投影计算键嵌入的能量估计，用于门控值聚合；MoPE用可学习的高斯窗波浪函数取代固定正弦编码，实现动态的位置-频率联合局部化。

Result: 在TinyShakespeare数据集上，EGA单独提升0.092验证损失（相对于标准注意力），比基准提升0.103；MoPE单独略差（-0.032）；二者组合达到+0.119，超过两者之和，体现显著超加性。多轮独立训练中结果一致。消融实验表明，受约束的先验方法普遍表现较差，而可学习的互补组件产生协同增益。

Conclusion: 能量敏感性和尺度选择性局部性是互补的归纳偏置，二者共同作用时能显著提升模型性能。可学习的组件优于预设结构的先验，且它们之间的交互具有超加性，提示未来应探索更灵活、自适应的注意力机制设计。

Abstract: Standard transformer attention computes pairwise token similarity but treats all tokens as equally salient and all positions as equally local, regardless of the informational structure of the input. We identify two complementary inductive biases that standard attention lacks: energy salience (which tokens concentrate informational energy, learned end-to-end without explicit frequency decomposition) and scale-selective locality (how far positional influence extends at each frequency, implemented via Morlet wavelet encoding). We address both with two simple components. Energy-Gated Attention (EGA) gates value aggregation by a learned energy estimate of key token embeddings, computed via a single linear projection; it selects what to attend to. Morlet Positional Encoding (MoPE) replaces fixed sinusoidal encodings with learned Gaussian-windowed wavelets that adapt the joint position-frequency localization to the corpus; it specifies where attention operates at each scale. On TinyShakespeare, EGA alone achieves +0.092 validation loss improvement over standard attention (+0.103 over Phase 1-3 baseline); MoPE alone is -0.032 (below baseline as a standalone encoding); but their combination achieves +0.119 -- more than the sum of parts. This superadditivity, observed across two independent training runs, is the central empirical finding: salience and locality are complementary inductive biases, each addressing a gap the other cannot fill alone. Ablations confirm that structured spectral priors (Morlet wavelet gates, scale-initialized heads, fixed sinusoidal PE) consistently underperform their unconstrained learned counterparts, while complementary learned components interact superadditively. All experiments are at small scale (<=6M parameters, character-level benchmarks, single seed); larger-scale multi-seed validation is the most important direction for future work.

### [202] [Balancing Plasticity and Stability with Fast and Slow Successor Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26357)
*Raymond Chua,Doina Precup,Blake Richards*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了深度强化学习（RL）在持续非平稳环境中的适应能力，通过修改3D Miniworld和MuJoCo环境引入自然的、渐进式的环境变化。研究发现，强调稳定性的方法（如突触巩固）优于强调可塑性的方法（如参数重置）。进一步实验表明，以成功特征（SFs）为巩固目标比以Q值更有效，尤其当在多个时间尺度上稳定SF时效果最佳。结果支持在渐进式变化环境中，稳定性比可塑性更重要，且多时间尺度的预测表征巩固是一种高效策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 改造3D Miniworld和MuJoCo环境以引入自然的、持续的非平稳性；对比不同方法在持续变化环境下的表现，包括基于突触巩固的稳定性策略和基于参数重置的可塑性策略；进一步探究以成功特征（SFs）作为巩固目标的效果，并分析多时间尺度对巩固性能的影响。

Result: 在持续非平稳环境中，强调稳定性的方法（如突触巩固）显著优于强调可塑性的方法；将神经启发的突触巩固应用于成功特征（SFs）能带来更优性能；特别是在多时间尺度上稳定SF时，表现最佳。

Abstract: A hallmark of intelligence is the ability to adapt in non-stationary environments, yet deep Reinforcement Learning (RL) agents often struggle in such settings. Prior studies introduce non-stationarity through abrupt shifts in features or dynamics, whereas real-world environments often evolve gradually through continual drift. This distinction has important implications for the "stability-plasticity dilemma" in RL, as abrupt task changes may demand more plasticity than naturalistic settings. To address this, we modify existing 3D Miniworld and MuJoCo environments to incorporate naturalistic, continual non-stationarity, and use them to examine how stability and adaptation affect performance under continuous environmental change. We find that methods favoring stability, such as synaptic consolidation, outperform approaches focused on plasticity, such as parameters resetting. Motivated by this result, and prior evidence that Successor Features (SFs) reduce interference, we investigate whether SFs are better consolidation targets than Q-values. Across both environments, applying neuro-inspired synaptic consolidation to SFs yields superior performance on continually changing settings. Moreover, consolidation is most effective when SFs are stabilized across multiple timescales, which capture complementary aspects of gradual environmental change. Together, these results suggest that stability is more critical in continual learning when changes are gradual, and that multi-timescale consolidation of predictive representations is an effective approach.

### [203] [Online Learning on Hidden-Convex Losses via Algorithmic Equivalence: Optimal Regret, Geometric Barrier, and Bandit Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26373)
*Anas Barakat,Andreas Kontogiannis,Vasilis Pollatos,Ioannis Panageas,Antonios Varvitsiotis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有隐藏凸损失的对抗性在线学习，即非凸损失在非线性重参数化后变为凸。Ghai、Lu 和 Hazan（2022）证明，在几何和光滑性假设下，在线梯度下降（OGD）在这些非凸损失上近似模拟了在线镜像下降（OMD）在底层凸损失上的行为，实现了 $\mathcal{O}(T^{2/3})$ 的遗憾。他们未解决的问题是：能否在该隐藏凸设置中恢复对抗性凸优化中的最优 $Θ(\sqrt{T})$ 遗憾。本文正面回答了这一问题，通过更精细的离散时间算法等价性论证，证明在相同假设下 OGD 可达到 $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{T})$ 遗憾，匹配对抗性凸优化的最优最坏情况率。此外，本文澄清了实现这种算法等价性的几何条件，将原先的对角雅可比充分条件替换为必要且充分的海森兼容性条件，从而扩大了允许的重参数化类。我们还给出了一个下界，表明海森兼容性假设是必要的；当该条件不成立时，构造了一个光滑重参数化及对抗性损失序列，使得 OGD 遭受 $Ω(T)$ 遗憾。最后，我们将分析扩展到单点带索引反馈，证明使用球形平滑的带索引 OGD 实现 $\mathcal{O}(T^{3/4})$ 期望遗憾，匹配其在凸损失下的经典速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决 Ghai、Lu 和 Hazan（2022）提出的开放问题：是否可以在隐藏凸损失设置中恢复对抗性凸优化的最优 $\\Theta(\\sqrt{T})$ 遗憾？同时明确实现算法等价性的几何条件，提升理论适用范围，并拓展至带索引反馈场景。

Method: 采用更精细的离散时间算法等价性分析，引入海森兼容性条件替代原有的对角雅可比条件，结合构造反例建立下界，并将结果推广至带索引反馈情形，使用球形平滑方法分析带索引 OGD 的性能。

Result: 证明了在线梯度下降（OGD）在隐藏凸损失下可实现 $\\mathcal{O}(\\sqrt{T})$ 遗憾，达到对抗性凸优化的最优率；提出并验证了海森兼容性为必要且充分条件；构造反例表明该条件不可或缺；在带索引反馈下，带索引 OGD 达到 $\\mathcal{O}(T^{3/4})$ 期望遗憾，与经典结果一致。

Conclusion: 本文解决了隐藏凸在线学习中的关键开放问题，证明了 OGD 在适当条件下可实现最优 $\\mathcal{O}(\\sqrt{T})$ 遗憾，明确了几何条件的本质要求，并将分析拓展至带索引反馈场景，显著提升了理论深度与应用广度。

Abstract: We study adversarial online learning with hidden-convex losses, i.e., nonconvex losses that become convex after a nonlinear reparameterization. Ghai, Lu and Hazan (2022) proved that, under geometric and smoothness assumptions, online gradient descent (OGD) on such nonconvex losses approximately simulates online mirror descent (OMD) on the underlying convex losses with a suitable regularizer, yielding $\mathcal{O}(T^{2/3})$ regret. They left open whether the optimal $Θ(\sqrt{T})$ regret from online convex optimization can be recovered in this hidden-convex setting. We answer this question affirmatively. More specifically, via a sharper discrete-time algorithmic equivalence argument, we prove that OGD achieves $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{T})$ regret under the same assumptions, matching the optimal worst-case rate for adversarial online convex optimization. We also address another open question of Ghai, Lu and Hazan (2022) by clarifying the geometry required for this algorithmic equivalence. We replace the diagonal-Jacobian sufficient condition with a necessary-and-sufficient Hessian compatibility condition, thereby expanding the class of admissible reparameterizations. We complement our tight regret bound with a lower bound showing that the Hessian compatibility assumption is essential for OGD; when it fails, we construct a smooth reparameterization and an adversarial sequence of hidden-convex losses for which OGD suffers $Ω(T)$ regret. Finally, we extend our analysis to one-point bandit feedback and prove a $\mathcal{O}(T^{3/4})$ expected regret bound for bandit OGD with spherical smoothing, matching its classical rate on convex losses.

</details>


### [204] [Function-Valued Causal Influence in Nonlinear Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26408)
*Valentina V. Kuskova,Dmitry Zaytsev,Michael Coppedge*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出在时间序列因果发现中，使用非线性机器学习模型时，仅依赖标量边权重会掩盖模型实际学习到的状态依赖函数。作者提出基于个体条件期望的框架，直接估计函数值因果影响，并通过合成实验和民主发展案例研究证明，标量方法会忽略关键的非线性、异质性和非对称因果结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前时间序列因果发现多依赖标量边得分来总结非线性模型的结果，但这种做法忽略了模型真正学习到的状态依赖函数特性，导致信息丢失，无法揭示复杂的因果动态。

Method: 提出函数值因果影响的形式化定义，采用神经加性向量自回归（NAVAR）作为代表性架构，结合个体条件期望（ICE）方法直接从训练好的模型中估计因果响应函数。

Result: 合成实验显示，具有相似标量得分的边可能表现出截然不同的函数行为，如单调、阈值、饱和或符号变化；真实案例研究揭示了传统方法遗漏的制度特定与非对称因果结构。

Conclusion: 标量因果得分构成严重的信息瓶颈，应转向函数值因果分析以更准确地理解复杂时间序列中的动态因果关系。

Abstract: Causal discovery in time series is increasingly performed using nonlinear machine-learning models, yet the resulting causal relationships are almost always summarized by scalar edge scores. We argue that this practice obscures the true object learned by nonlinear autoregressive models: a state-dependent function whose effect varies across regimes, magnitudes, and contexts. We formalize function-valued causal influence for additive, contribution-decomposable architectures and show that scalar causal scores constitute a severe information bottleneck, conflating between-state variation with within-state residual noise. Using Neural Additive Vector Autoregression as a representative architecture, we introduce a practical framework based on Individual Conditional Expectation for estimating causal response functions directly from trained models. Through controlled synthetic experiments, we demonstrate that edges with indistinguishable scalar scores can exhibit qualitatively different functional behaviors, including monotonic, thresholded, saturating, and sign-changing effects. An applied case study on democratic development further shows that function-valued analysis reveals regime-specific and asymmetric causal structure systematically missed by score-centric approaches.

The formulation enables fast ODE-based sampling and flexible conditioning over heterogeneous event schedules.   <summary>Details</summary>

Despite showing positive results in data-rich regimes, they often fail to outperform significantly smaller supervised models in low-resource settings compared to fully supervised models. We provide a mechanistic account of this shortcoming, attributing it to a fundamental mismatch between reconstruction-based pretext tasks and the idiosyncratic spectral structure of EEG signals, which decompose into distinct high-power aperiodic and low-power oscillatory components. Using controlled, synthetically-generated EEG inputs, we demonstrate that EEG foundation model embeddings are biased to capture the aperiodic components of the EEG signal while under-representing oscillatory components, particularly at higher frequencies. Additionally, linear probe evaluations on real-world BCI datasets further reveal that embeddings encode subject identity more strongly than task-relevant information, thereby reinforcing the low-frequency and aperiodic component bias in foundation model embeddings trained primarily on reconstruction based objectives. Together, these findings elucidate a failure mode in reconstruction based EEG foundation models and motivate future work to incorporate auxiliary losses explicitly targeting high-frequency oscillatory structure as a path toward more capable and generalizable EEG representations.

However, existing GCN-based methods suffer from the fundamental problem of contamination propagation, where anomalous nodes pollute the representations of their neighbors through message passing, leading to degraded detection performance. In this paper, we propose DDGAD, a novel diffusion-based graph anomaly detection framework that leverages trajectory dynamics to distinguish normal and anomalous nodes. Our key insight is that normal nodes exhibit consistent and stable representation trajectories under the coupled effects of diffusion regularization and reliability-aware neighborhood consensus, while anomalous nodes exhibit unstable and conflicting dynamics due to the directional disagreement between the global manifold prior and locally contaminated message passing. To mitigate contamination propagation, we introduce a distributed reliability-aware consensus refinement mechanism and define three complementary anomaly signals: neighbor inconsistency, reliability weight, and dynamical conflict energy. We further provide a preliminary theoretical analysis on normal node stability under the coupled dynamics. These signals collectively characterize anomalous behaviors from the perspectives of local inconsistency, consensus reliability, and dynamical instability. Extensive experiments on five real-world datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework.

### [209] [MuCon: Clipped Muon Updates for LLM Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26459)
*Albert Yi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了MuCon优化器中奇异值裁剪步骤的近似问题，提出在不进行完整稠密SVD的情况下实现裁剪的可行性。通过两个精确恒等式（极坐标/绝对值公式和标量根公式）分析了数值障碍：接近裁剪阈值的奇异值会导致符号判断困难和求解病态。因此，矩阵函数方法需结合稳定极分解或平方根原语，或在裁剪边界附近引入显式正则化以保证数值稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在避免全量稠密奇异值分解（SVD）的前提下，对MuCon优化器中的奇异值裁剪步骤进行高效近似，以提升计算效率并保持数值稳定性。

Method: 利用两个数学恒等式：一是极分解与绝对值的关系，二是标量根形式导出的有理牛顿滤波器，用于逼近裁剪后的半正定因子；同时分析其在奇异值接近阈值时的数值缺陷。

Result: 证明了仅使用矩阵函数方法在临界区域存在数值不稳定性，必须结合稳定的极分解或平方根计算工具，或在裁剪边界处引入显式正则化才能有效应用。

Conclusion: MuCon的裁剪步骤虽可理论近似，但实际实现依赖于数值稳定的极分解或正则化策略，否则将因奇异值邻近阈值引发的病态问题而失效。

Abstract: Muon-style optimizers take a matrix-valued momentum or preconditioned update $B = U \operatorname{diag}(σ_1,\ldots,σ_r) V^\top$ and replace it with its canonical partial polar factor $\operatorname{Pol}(B) = U V^\top$. This maps every nonzero singular value to one. MuCon is the clipped-Muon variant studied here: it applies singular-value clipping to the same Muon matrix, $D^{\mathrm{MuCon}}\_τ(B) = \operatorname{MClip}\_τ(B) = U \operatorname{diag}\bigl(\min\{σ\_i,τ\}\bigr) V^\top, \qquad τ> 0$. Thus, $\operatorname{MClip}\_τ$ denotes the mathematical clipping operator, while MuCon denotes the optimizer primitive that substitutes this clipped direction for Muon's polar direction. The Muon/MuCon scaling parameterization used in this work is called $\text{SpectralP}$: it is the hidden-matrix scaling recipe under which polar Muon or clipped MuCon directions are applied. The map $\operatorname{MClip}\_τ$ is the Frobenius projection onto the spectral-norm ball $\{X : \|X\|_2 \le τ\}$: it leaves singular values at or below $τ$ unchanged and modifies only the violating singular directions. This paper asks when the MuCon clipping step can be approximated without a full dense SVD. We record two exact identities, a polar/absolute-value formula and a scalar-root formulation leading to a rational Newton filter for the clipped positive-semidefinite factor, and identify the numerical obstruction common to both: singular values near the threshold make sign decisions and rational solves ill-conditioned. Matrix-function methods are therefore useful only when paired with stable polar/square-root primitives or explicit regularization near the clipping boundary.

</details>

### [212] [The Stability of Singular Distribution: A Spectral Perspective on the Two-Phase Dynamics of Language Model Pre-training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26489)
*Hongtao Zhang,Wenjie Zhou,Chenxi Jia,Wei Chen,Xueqi Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大语言模型预训练中的一个普遍现象——奇异值分布稳定性（SoSD），即在训练初期，归一化奇异值谱即趋于稳定，尽管参数矩阵仍在持续演化。这一现象与损失下降的慢速阶段高度同步，广泛存在于多种架构（如GPT-2、LLaMA）和训练设置中。通过简化Transformer分析，证明权重范数增长会引发早期的SoSD阈值，此后损失下降速率受奇异值分布变化的理论限制。研究进一步从谱视角解释了WSD和Muon等优化策略的有效性，表明它们通过调节SoSD尺度实现更高效的预训练动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解大语言模型预训练中为何会出现先快后慢的损失下降轨迹，特别是慢速阶段的成因，以揭示其内在机制并指导高效训练策略的设计。

Result: SoSD在预训练早期即出现，并与慢速下降阶段一致；权重范数增长导致早期达到SoSD阈值，从而限制后续损失下降速度；不同优化策略（如WSD、Muon）可通过调节SoSD尺度提升训练效率。

Conclusion: 奇异值分布稳定性（SoSD）是理解大语言模型预训练动态的关键机制，为优化策略设计提供了新的谱分析视角，有助于实现更高效、更可预测的预训练过程。

Abstract: Large language model pre-training typically exhibits a two-phase trajectory: a fast initial loss drop followed by a prolonged slow improvement. We identify an underlying spectral phenomenon, Stability of Singular Distribution (SoSD), where the trace-normalized singular value spectrum stabilizes early, even as parameter matrices continue to evolve. We demonstrate that synchronization between SoSD and the slow-descent regime is widely observed across diverse architectures (GPT-2, LLaMA) and settings, including various schedules (Step-wise, WSD, Cosine Decay), weight decays, and optimizers (AdamW, Muon). By analyzing a simplified Transformer, we prove that growing weight norms inevitably precipitate an early SoSD threshold, after which the rate of loss decrease becomes theoretically bounded by the variation in the singular distribution. We further interpret strategies like WSD and Muon through their ability to modulate the SoSD scale, offering a spectral lens for understanding efficient pre-training dynamics.

### [213] [Beyond Pairwise Preferences: Listwise Reward-Aware Alignment for Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26491)
*Austin Wang,Jiaqi Han,Stefano Ermon,Yisong Yue*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Diffusion LAIR 是一种奖励感知的列表偏好优化方法，用于对齐文本到图像扩散模型。它通过将一组候选图像的奖励分数转换为中心化的优势权重，优化隐式奖励上的加权回归目标，并引入二次惩罚项以控制隐式奖励的大小，从而在不依赖成对比较的情况下利用所有候选图像的信息，同时保持保守性。实验表明，该方法在 SD1.5 和 SDXL 上优于现有基线，在文本到图像生成、组合生成和图像编辑任务中表现更优。

Method: Diffusion LAIR 将每个提示下的多候选图像奖励分数转化为中心化优势权重，构建基于隐式奖励（当前模型相对于固定参考模型的去噪损失改进）的加权回归目标，并加入二次正则项以控制隐式奖励的幅度，实现列表级偏好学习。

Result: 在 SD1.5 和 SDXL 模型上，Diffusion LAIR 在文本到图像生成、组合生成和图像编辑等多个基准测试中均显著优于现有偏好优化基线方法，证明其有效性与优越性。

Conclusion: Diffusion LAIR 通过列表级奖励感知优化，有效利用了多候选图像中的丰富信息，同时保持训练稳定性与保守性，为扩散模型对齐提供了高效且可扩展的新范式。

Abstract: Preference optimization has emerged as an efficient alternative to online reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) for aligning text-to-image diffusion models. However, existing methods largely reduce supervision to binary pairwise comparisons. This pairwise reduction is limiting when training data naturally contains multiple candidate images for the same prompt, and when continuous reward scores can provide richer information than a single winner-loser label. To address these limitations, we propose Diffusion LAIR, a reward-aware listwise preference optimization method for diffusion models. For each prompt, LAIR converts reward scores across a group of candidate images into centered advantage weights, then optimizes an advantage-weighted regression objective on the implicit reward, defined as the denoising-loss improvement of the current model over a fixed reference model, with a quadratic penalty that regularizes the magnitude of the implicit reward. The resulting objective uses all candidates simultaneously rather than selecting pairs, and remains conservative by explicitly controlling the magnitude of the implicit reward. The LAIR objective admits a bounded closed-form optimum in implicit-reward space, clarifying how the regularization strength controls the magnitude of the preference update. Experiments show that Diffusion LAIR outperforms strong preference optimization baselines on SD1.5 and SDXL across text-to-image generation, compositional generation, and image editing benchmarks.

</details>


### [214] [Dense2MoE: Pushing the Pareto Frontier of On-Device LLMs via Unified Pruning and Upcycling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26496)
*Fengfa Li,Hongjin Ji,Yifeng Ding,Lei Ren,Chen Wei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Dense2MoE提出一种统一剪枝与升维的框架，通过层融合技术，基于硬件屋顶线理论，修剪冗余层中的注意力模块，并将多层感知机（MLP）重用为MoE专家，从而在保持模型核心能力的同时减少活跃参数，提升设备端推理效率。仅需少量持续预训练即可将公开密集型大模型转化为设备就绪的MoE模型，在延迟-精度权衡上显著优于现有方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MoE模型训练成本高，而现有升维或剪枝方法存在参数冗余或准确率下降问题，亟需一种兼顾效率与性能的解决方案。

Method: 提出Dense2MoE框架，结合层融合（LF）与升维（UC），基于硬件屋顶线理论，系统性地剪枝带宽密集型注意力模块，同时将冗余层的MLP转换为MoE专家，实现参数高效利用与选择性令牌路由。

Conclusion: Dense2MoE成功解决了资源受限设备部署中模型效率与精度的矛盾，提供了一种高效、可扩展的从密集模型到MoE模型的转化路径。

Abstract: The Mixture of Experts MoE architecture is highly promising for resource constrained on device deployments yet training these models from scratch incurs prohibitive costs Current methods attempt to alleviate this by upcycling dense models into MoEs however they often introduce parameter redundancy that degrades inference efficiency Alternatively standard layer pruning mitigates redundancy but inevitably compromises model accuracy To resolve this dilemma we propose Dense2MoE a novel framework that unifies pruning and upcycling through Layer Fusion UpCycling LF UC Guided by hardware Roofline theory Dense2MoE systematically overcomes the inference memory wall by pruning bandwidth heavy attention modules from redundant layers while repurposing their Multi Layer Perceptrons MLPs into MoE experts This structural innovation preserves the models core capabilities and strictly limits active parameters via selective token routing With a modest continual pre training budget Dense2MoE efficiently converts publicly available dense LLMs into on device ready MoE models Extensive experiments demonstrate that Dense2MoE significantly advances the Pareto frontier for on device inference latency versus model accuracy outperforming dense baselines state of the art compression and standard upcycling methods

### [215] [Open-Weight LLM Fine-Tuning Defenses are Susceptible to Simple Attacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26526)
*Kevin Kuo,Chhavi Yadav,Virginia Smith*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了开放权重大语言模型的安全防护机制在面对非微调类攻击（如消融和预填充）时存在显著漏洞，这些攻击无需梯度优化即可大幅提升恶意行为的成功率。研究提出抗消融微调（ART）以增强防御能力，并强调应扩展评估手段以涵盖更广泛的攻击策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有针对开放权重大语言模型的防御措施假设有害行为需通过微调获得，但实际中模型本身已包含大量有害知识，因此需要评估是否存在无需微调即可通过越狱实现恶意使用的攻击方式。

Method: 采用两种低成本攻击方法——消融和预填充，不依赖梯度优化，在三个基准测试（BeaverTails、HarmBench、AdvBench）上评估其对受保护模型的有效性；并提出一种名为抗消融微调（ART）的新训练目标以增强鲁棒性。

Result: 消融与预填充攻击使受保护模型的攻击成功率从低于10%提升至16%-96%；引入ART后，这三种攻击及其组合的成功率降低10%-20%。

Conclusion: 开放权重模型的攻击面比以往认知更广，当前防御机制需纳入更多样化的攻击评估策略，而不仅仅是对抗性微调。

Abstract: Recent defenses for safeguarding open-weight large language models (LLMs) are intended to prevent adversarial usage. Underlying these defenses is an assumption that new harmful behavior is learned through fine-tuning rather than elicited by jailbreaking the model. Yet, pretrained LLMs already encode substantial harmful knowledge across many domains, which raises an important question: can an adversary jailbreak safeguarded models, to achieve harmful usage without fine-tuning at all? In this paper, we show that open-weight safeguards are susceptible to simpler strategies that, despite being well known, have not been systematically evaluated against these safeguards. Specifically, we evaluate two low-cost attacks--abliteration and prefilling--that do not rely on gradient-based optimization. Across three harmfulness evaluation benchmarks (BeaverTails, HarmBench, and AdvBench), these attacks increase attack success rates against safeguarded open-weight models from below 10\% to a range of 16%-96%. To mitigate this vulnerability, we introduce abliteration-resistant tuning (ART), which incorporates an abliteration-based objective into training. ART can be layered onto existing defenses and reduces the success rates of abliteration, prefilling, and their combination by 10%-20%. These findings indicate that the attack surface for open-weight models is broader than previously characterized, and that evaluations of safeguarding defenses should incorporate a more diverse set of attack strategies beyond adversarial fine-tuning.

Abstract: Generative models have emerged as a powerful paradigm for solving physics systems and modeling complex spatiotemporal dynamics. In this work, we introduce Recursive Flow Matching (RecFM), a generative framework for forecasting complex spatiotemporal dynamics. RecFM enforces self-consistency to align trajectories across discretization scales, reducing discretization errors and improving performance across metrics for physics-based tasks. To our knowledge, this is the first method to achieve high-fidelity one- and few-step (2-4 step) dynamic generation for scientific systems with performance comparable to state-of-the-art multi-step solvers. Across challenging scientific benchmarks, RecFM achieves up to a 20$\times$ speedup over leading diffusion-based emulators while improving predictive accuracy. ### [217] [Aligning Few-Step Generative Models by Amortizing Sample-based Variational Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26552)
*Jaewoo Lee,Hyeongyu Kang,Dohyun Kim,Kyuil Sim,Woocheol Shin,Minsu Kim,Taeyoung Yun,Jeongjae Lee,Sanghyeok Choi,Tabitha Edith Lee,Jongchul Ye,Jinkyoo Park*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对齐框架通常依赖于限制性假设，如可计算似然、特定的常微分方程/随机微分方程求解器或特定模型家族。为克服这些限制，提出一种仅需样本访问的通用对齐方法。

Method: 将对齐问题建模为从以参考分布为锚点的奖励倾斜分布中采样；采用基于样本的变分推断方法——Stein变分梯度下降；通过固定点回归将粒子更新过程高效地映射至生成器参数。

Result: 在机器人操作任务中，FAV在56个离线和30个离线到在线强化学习任务上优于现有策略提取基线；在图像生成领域，成功对齐多种少步生成模型（如GAN、漂移模型、一致性模型、流模型），支持从ImageNet-256到1024²的文本到图像合成。

Abstract: Aligning a few-step generative model is challenging, since existing alignment frameworks typically rely on restrictive assumptions: a tractable likelihood, a specific ODE/SDE solver, or a particular model family. We introduce FAV, Few-step Generative Models Alignment via Sample-based Variational Inference, a general alignment framework that requires only sample access to the generator and the reference distribution. We cast alignment as sampling from a reward-tilted distribution anchored to a reference distribution. We leverage Stein Variational Gradient Descent as a sample-based variational inference scheme and amortize its particle updates into the generator parameters via fixed-point regression. We evaluate FAV on two domains: robotics manipulation and image generator alignment. On generative policy alignment for robotic manipulation, FAV outperforms prevailing policy extraction baselines across 56 offline and 30 offline-to-online RL tasks. For image generator alignment, FAV fine-tunes diverse few-step backbones, including GAN, drifting model, consistency models, and flow maps, scaling from ImageNet-$256$ to 1024$^2$ text-to-image synthesis. Code is available at https://github.com/Jaewoopudding/FAV.

### [218] [Auditing and Fixing Economic Validity in Tabular Foundation Models for Discrete Choice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26559)

Method: 提出两阶段适配器：第一阶段使用受经济理论约束的标准选择模型（如Logit）进行参数估计；第二阶段固定这些参数，引入一个修正模块，利用基础模型的预测作为额外信息进行微调，从而实现精度与经济一致性的平衡。

Conclusion: 通过将基础模型预测嵌入效用最大化框架，所提出的两阶段适配器成功结合了高准确率与严格的经济逻辑，为决策支持系统提供了更可靠、可解释的预测工具。

Abstract: Tabular foundation models achieve strong accuracy on choice prediction tasks, but their predictions often violate the economic logic those tasks require: raising a price sometimes increases predicted demand, and implied willingness-to-pay estimates are frequently negative or implausible. We propose a two-stage adapter that embeds foundation model predictions within a utility-maximization framework. In the first stage, we estimate a standard choice model whose parameters are constrained to obey economic theory. In the second stage, we freeze those parameters and train a correction term that incorporates the foundation model's predictions as additional information. The result is a model that inherits the foundation model's accuracy gains while guaranteeing monotonic price-demand relationships under policy perturbation and producing analytically computable trade-off measures. On two transportation datasets, the adapter recovers up to 13 percentage points of accuracy over a standard logit model while maintaining perfect economic consistency, something neither the raw foundation models nor conventional distillation achieve.

Abstract: We present Distribution-aware Conformal Prediction (DCP), a unified framework integrating probabilistic predictors like Monte Carlo dropout, deep ensembles, and quantile regression with score-agnostic conformal calibration to produce valid and efficient prediction intervals. Crucially, DCP's modular design facilitates plug-and-play experimentation with different predictor-score pairings, quantitatively supported by a newly introduced modified Winkler score that balances validity and efficiency by explicitly penalizing undercoverage. Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PGFedSplit 是一种新型个性化联邦学习框架，旨在解决客户端数据异构性下的性能下降问题。通过分拆架构和自适应聚合调度，该方法在保持全局泛化能力的同时增强了个性化适应能力，并利用本地与服务器端生成的合成表示提升在标签不平衡和类别缺失情况下的鲁棒性。实验表明，PGFedSplit 在多个基准数据集上均优于现有最先进方法，具有稳定的收敛性和优越的个性化表现。

Abstract: Federated learning enables collaborative model training without sharing raw data, but its performance can degrade substantially under heterogeneous client data distributions. A single global model often cannot satisfy diverse client requirements, so personalized federated learning has therefore been explored to improve client specific performance while preserving global generalization. Existing PFL methods often face a fundamental tradeoff in which stronger global sharing can undermine local specialization, whereas stronger local adaptation can lead to overfitting under limited data, label imbalance, and missing class scenarios. In this work, we propose PGFedSplit, a personalized federated learning framework that improves both personalization and global generalization under severe client heterogeneity. PGFedSplit adopts a split architecture and performs adaptive aggregation scheduling tailored to the roles of different model components, enabling stable knowledge sharing while maintaining client specific adaptation. Each client further leverages a mixture of locally extracted representations and synthetic representations generated from server side Gaussian statistics, improving robustness under label imbalance and missing class conditions. Extensive experiments on Fashion MNIST, CIFAR 10, CIFAR 100, and Tiny ImageNet demonstrate consistent improvements over state of the art PFL methods, with stable convergence and superior personalization in highly heterogeneous settings.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于多维评估标准的强化学习训练存在奖励极化问题，即使整体奖励高，某些维度仍可能表现严重不足，影响用户体验。

Method: 采用逆奖励投影机制估计各评估维度的饱和度，进而设计带有自适应重权重系数的最终目标函数，实现细粒度的奖励平衡。

Result: 在三种模型规模和六个基准测试中，Focal Reward在所有18个模型-基准组合中均优于最强静态聚合基线；消融与机制分析表明，性能提升源于对尚有改进空间维度的在线、饱和感知资源再分配。

Conclusion: Focal Reward有效缓解了多维评估下的奖励极化问题，提升了生成质量的均衡性与用户满意度，为大模型强化学习训练提供了更鲁棒的优化框架。

Abstract: The open-ended generation in LLMs usually requires multi-dimensional rubrics to adequately assess quality and guide the improvement of reinforcement learning. However, a critical dilemma inherent in this training paradigm is the imbalanced reward polarization along different rubric dimensions. Under this bottleneck, even if LLMs achieve relatively high rewards after training, they may still exhibit severe deficiencies in certain dimensions, leading to a direct deterioration in user experience. To address this problem, we propose Focal Reward, a novel objective to automatically balance the training of reinforcement learning under rubric-based rewards. Specifically, we first leverage an inverse reward projection mechanism to estimate the saturation degree of each criterion in the rubric, which forms the basis to calibrate the reward direction. Then, the final objective is designed with an automatically reweighting coefficient for each criterion to achieve the fine-grained balancing. Extensive experiments across three model scales and six benchmarks demonstrate that our Focal Reward method outperforms the strongest static aggregation baseline in all 18 model-benchmark comparisons. Rollout, mechanism, and ablation analyses further show that these gains arise from online, saturation-aware reallocation toward rubrics that still have room for improvement.

### [222] [On the Error-Correcting Effects of Stochasticity in Discrete Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26582)
*William Yuan,Sungwon Jeong,Amirali Aghazadeh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了马尔可夫转移中的随机性程度如何影响离散扩散模型的采样权衡。研究表明，高度确定性的转移收敛快但易累积误差，而更随机的转移收敛慢但能获得更高最终样本质量。通过信息论分析，作者发现冗余转移在状态间对称地交换质量，具有纠错效应，可证明收缩采样误差。基于此，提出一种新算法D CRS（离散蠕动与重启采样），通过交替进行前向和反向扩散过程注入可控随机性。实验表明，在低函数评估次数下，DCRS显著改善速度-质量权衡；在图像数据上，相比标准采样器减少高达10倍采样步数且保持良好质量；在语言任务中表现则取决于扰动过程和采样方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离散扩散模型在文本和图像生成中表现优异，但推理速度慢，需在采样效率与样本质量之间权衡。现有方法缺乏对随机性在采样过程中的作用的深入理解，因此亟需一种能有效控制随机性以优化采样性能的新机制。

Method: 提出基于信息论分析的理论框架，揭示冗余转移的纠错机制；设计并实现离散蠕动与重启采样（DCRS）算法，通过交替前向与反向扩散过程引入可控随机性，从而调节采样路径的稳定性和质量。

Result: 在合成数据集和大规模基准测试中，DCRS在低函数评估次数下显著提升采样效率与质量的平衡；图像生成任务中可减少最多10倍采样步数，同时保持高质量输出；语言任务中表现出依赖于具体扰动与采样策略的复杂行为。

Conclusion: 随机性在离散扩散模型的采样过程中起关键作用，适度的随机性可通过冗余转移实现误差校正。DCRS通过精心设计的随机化策略，在保证样本质量的前提下大幅提高采样效率，为离散扩散模型的高效推理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion models achieve strong performance in text and image generation, but their inference remains slow and must inherently balance sampling efficiency and sample quality. In this work, we present a systematic study of how the \emph{degree of stochasticity} in Markov transitions governs the sampling tradeoff. We show that highly deterministic transitions converge rapidly but suffer from error accumulation, while more stochastic transitions converge more slowly yet can achieve higher final sample quality. Using an information-theoretic analysis, we identify the underlying mechanism as an error-correcting effect induced by \emph{redundant transitions} that symmetrically exchange mass between states, and show that these transitions can provably contract sampling errors. Motivated by this analysis, we propose \emph{Discrete Churn and Restart Sampling} (DCRS), a novel inference algorithm that injects controlled stochasticity by alternating between forward and reverse diffusion processes. Experiments on synthetic datasets and large-scale benchmarks show that DCRS improves the speed-quality tradeoff in the low number of function evaluations regime. On image datasets, DCRS achieves up to a $10\times$ reduction in sampling steps compared to standard samplers while maintaining competitive sample quality, whereas on language benchmarks, we observe more nuanced behavior depending on the corruption process and sampling procedure.

### [223] [Near-Optimal Regret in Adversarial Kernel Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26585)
*Yu-Jie Zhang,Hao Qiu,Jonathan Scarlett,Kevin Jamieson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究对抗性核函数带宽问题，提出一种基于正则化重要性加权损失估计器的指数权重算法，并引入显式校正项以消除正则化带来的偏差。主要结果表明，遗憾度上界为 $\widetilde{O}\big(\sqrt{T\, d_*(λ)\,\log|{X}|}\big)$，其中 $d_*(λ)$ 是衡量核函数复杂性的有效维度。该结果在对数因子内与随机核函数带宽问题中的已知最优率一致。对于 $\mathbb{R}^d$ 上的 Matérn$(ν,d)$ 核函数，其遗憾度上界为 $\widetilde{O}\big(T^{(ν+d)/(2ν+d)}\big)$，优于先前最佳结果，并且无需假设对手为秩一形式。该速率与已知最优随机核带宽问题速率一致，且与近期下界结果仅差一个 $\log T$ 因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种基于正则化重要性加权损失估计器的指数权重算法，引入显式校正项以消除正则化导致的偏差，结合有效维度 $d_*(λ)$ 分析算法性能。

Result: 遗憾度上界为 $\widetilde{O}\big(\sqrt{T\, d_*(λ)\,\log|{X}|}\big)$，对于 Matérn$(ν,d)$ 核函数，具体为 $\widetilde{O}\big(T^{(ν+d)/(2ν+d)}\big)$，优于已有结果并匹配最优速率。

Conclusion: 所提算法在对抗性核函数带宽问题中实现了接近最优的遗憾率，适用于广泛核函数，且无需强对手假设，显著提升了理论性能和适用范围。

Abstract: We study the adversarial kernel bandit problem, in which the loss at each round is induced by an arbitrary bounded element of a reproducing kernel Hilbert space (RKHS). We propose an exponential-weights algorithm built on a regularized importance-weighted loss estimator, together with an explicit correction term that cancels the bias introduced by the regularization. Our main result bounds the regret by $\widetilde{O}\big(\sqrt{T\, d_*(λ)\,\log|{X}|}\big)$, where $d_*(λ)$ is a widely-adopted notion of effective dimension that captures the complexity of the kernel. Up to logarithmic factors, this matches the known rate achieved in the related stochastic kernel bandit problem. A notable application is the Matérn$(ν,d)$ kernel with smoothness parameter $ν$ on $\mathbb{R}^d$, for which our bound specializes to $\widetilde{O}\big(T^{(ν+d)/(2ν+d)}\big)$, improving over the best-known prior rate of Chatterji et al. [2019] while simultaneously removing the rank-one adversary assumption required by their analysis. Moreover, this rate is the same as the known optimal rate for stochastic kernel bandits, and also matches a lower bound from concurrent work up to a $\log T$ factor.

Subgroup analyses included sex, age, residence, maternal education, and wealth. Feature importance was estimated using SHAP.
  TabPFN outperformed classical models in low-data regimes (<200 samples), showing higher discrimination and better calibration. LOCO performance was stable (0.58-0.69), driven by country context. Reverse-LOCO showed asymmetric transferability. Subgroup performance was consistent with no systematic demographic bias. SHAP identified child age, altitude, and height-for-age z-score as dominant predictors, followed by wealth and maternal education.
  Performance in childhood anemia prediction is driven more by population variation than model choice. TabPFN provides advantages in low-resource settings through improved discrimination and calibration, highlighting foundation models as promising tools for data-scarce global health prediction.

### [225] [Spend Your Rollouts Where It Counts: Rollout Allocation for Group-Based RL Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26606)
*Woojeong Kim,Ziyi Yang,Jing Nathan Yan,Jialu Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Pilot-Commit 是一种预算感知的采样分配框架，用于组级强化学习后训练。它通过分阶段评估提示信息量，将计算资源集中于高价值提示，显著降低采样成本并提升训练效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前组级策略优化方法在在线、在线策略设置下存在采样浪费问题，尤其在奖励分布坍缩的提示上仍分配大量资源，导致计算效率低下。需要一种动态、高效的方法来识别和聚焦于真正有学习信号的提示。

Method: Pilot-Commit 将过程分为两个阶段：首先在‘试点阶段’使用少量采样估算每个提示的信息量；随后在‘执行阶段’将剩余采样预算集中分配给高信息量提示，低信息量提示则跳过，实现预算的智能分配。

Result: 在多个数学推理基准和不同规模模型（1.5B 到 14B 参数）上，Pilot-Commit 在保持与基线相当准确率的前提下，显著降低了采样开销，比 GRPO 快 1.9 倍，比 DAPO 快 4.0 倍（以累计采样数衡量）。

Conclusion: Pilot-Commit 有效解决了组级 RL 后训练中的采样效率瓶颈，通过在线估计提示信息量并动态分配预算，实现了更高训练效率和更低计算成本，是大规模语言模型后训练中极具潜力的优化框架。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) is the dominant paradigm for post-training large language models. However, in the online, on-policy setting, rollout generation dominates the computational cost of training. Group-based policy optimization methods compute advantages from multiple rollouts per prompt, yet they indiscriminately allocate budget to prompts with collapsed reward distributions, wasting expensive rollouts on negligible learning signals. We demonstrate that group-based updates are most effective in regimes of high reward variance. Since the policy evolves throughout training, prompt informativeness must be estimated online rather than precomputed, but exhaustively evaluating every prompt is computationally prohibitive. We introduce Pilot-Commit, a budget-aware rollout allocation framework for group-based RL post-training. Pilot-Commit decouples prompt evaluation from exploitation: a pilot stage estimates per-prompt informativeness using a fraction of the budget, and the remaining rollouts are allocated to high-leverage prompts while low-signal prompts are skipped. Across multiple math reasoning benchmarks and model scales from 1.5B to 14B parameters, Pilot-Commit matches baseline accuracy with significantly lower sampling costs, reaching target accuracy up to $1.9\times$ faster than GRPO and $4.0\times$ faster than DAPO in cumulative rollouts.

### [226] [PIDM-DP: Physics-Informed Diffusion with Dormand-Prince Integration for Chaotic System Identification and State Reconstruction across Multiple Dynamical Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26619)
*Shailendra Dabral*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PIDM-DP integrates a differentiable 5th-order ODE solver into a diffusion model to reconstruct chaotic system trajectories from noisy, sparse data. It uses physics-informed guidance with adaptive weighting to avoid gradient explosions and outperforms baselines on complex systems.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Reconstructing continuous state trajectories from sparse, noisy observations in chaotic systems is challenging due to sensitivity to initial conditions and numerical instabilities. Existing methods struggle with stiff systems and fail to preserve underlying physical laws.

Method: The paper proposes PIDM-DP, which embeds a fully differentiable Dormand-Prince (DP-RK45) integrator within the reverse sampling loop of a Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Model (DDPM). Physics residuals are back-propagated via automatic differentiation, enforcing adherence to governing equations at 5th-order accuracy. A linear-scheduled guidance mechanism gradually increases physics weight to prevent instability in stiff systems.

Result: PIDM-DP achieves up to 15.4× lower RMSE than unconstrained diffusion across five benchmark chaotic systems (Lorenz, Rössler, Hyperchaotic, Lorenz-96, Rabinovich-Fabrikant) under 10% observation density and Gaussian noise (σ=0.05). It significantly outperforms EnKF on stiff systems and shows superior performance on out-of-distribution Rabinovich-Fabrikant data (RMSE: 0.1097 vs. 0.9443 for diffusion, p<0.001). Topological analysis confirms preserved chaotic dynamics via Lyapunov estimation.

Conclusion: PIDM-DP enables accurate, physically consistent reconstruction of chaotic trajectories from sparse, noisy observations by combining differentiable ODE integration with diffusion modeling, offering robustness to stiffness and improved generalization to unseen dynamics.

Abstract: Reconstructing continuous state trajectories of chaotic dynamical systems from sparse, noisy observations remains a fundamental open problem in nonlinear science. We introduce the Physics-Informed Diffusion Model with Dormand-Prince Integration (PIDM-DP), which embeds a fully differentiable 5th-order Dormand-Prince (DP-RK45) ODE integrator directly into the reverse sampling loop of a Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Model (DDPM). At each denoising step, physics residuals are back-propagated via automatic differentiation, constraining every generated trajectory to satisfy the system's governing equations to 5th-order accuracy. A linear-scheduled guidance mechanism that ramps the physics weight from zero at high noise levels to its full value near the clean-data limit prevents the gradient explosions that cause naive physics-informed approaches to fail on stiff systems with Jacobian eigenvalues of order $O(10^3)$. Evaluated across five benchmark systems of increasing complexity 3D Lorenz, 3D Rössler, 5D Hyperchaotic, 20D Lorenz-96, and the stiff 3D Rabinovich-Fabrikant at 10% observation density with additive Gaussian noise ($σ=0.05$), PIDM-DP achieves reconstruction RMSE improvements of up to $15.4\times$ over an unconstrained diffusion baseline and decisively outperforms the Ensemble Kalman Filter on stiff systems where ensemble covariance collapses. On the Rabinovich-Fabrikant out-of-distribution benchmark, PIDM-DP attains RMSE $0.1097 \pm 0.0269$ versus $0.9443 \pm 0.5288$ (unconstrained diffusion, $8.6\times$ worse) and $0.3561 \pm 0.3040$ (EnKF, $3.2\times$ worse), with $p<0.001$ in paired Wilcoxon tests ($N = 30$). Topological validation via the Rosenstein Lyapunov estimator confirms that PIDM-DP preserves the chaotic invariant measure.

Abstract: Diffusion Transformers (DiT) achieve strong performance in image generation but incur substantial inference costs. While prior work has reduced this cost via quantization and distillation, semi-structured sparsity, which can nearly halve FLOPs, remains underexplored. A key reason is that most existing approaches focus on weight sparsification, and pruning 50% of the weights can remove critical model capacity and degrade generation quality. Our study, however, shows that DiT activations are intrinsically sparse and significantly more robust to N:M semi-structured sparsification than weights. Motivated by this observation, we advocate a paradigm shift from weight sparsification to activation sparsification. We propose RT-Lynx, which applies N:M sparsification to activations and incorporates error-compensation techniques to mitigate accuracy loss.
