### [278] [Anchor: Mitigating Artifact Drift in Agent Benchmark Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26321)
*Maksim Ivanov,Abhijay Rana*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Anchor任务生成管道，将企业业务流程规范形式化为约束优化程序，实现自然语言指令、环境配置、求解器认证的真值解和基于状态的验证器的联合生成。该方法可控制难度并确保最优解已知，避免了因流程松散耦合导致的“人工制品漂移”问题。基于此构建了包含300个长期任务的ERP-Bench基准，用于评估智能体在采购与制造工作流中的表现。结果显示，生成参数能有效预测任务难度，而前沿模型仅在17.4%的试验中达到完全最优解。整体上，Anchor与ERP-Bench为构建可审计的企业级智能体评估环境提供了可行方案，并已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有企业级任务训练与评估环境难以平衡真实性、可验证性和规模，常因指令、环境、规则和验证器由松散耦合流程生成，导致任务不可解、奖励可操纵或不一致，即‘人工制品漂移’问题。

Method: 提出Anchor任务生成管道，将领域专家定义的业务流程转化为约束优化程序，从单一参数化规格中联合生成自然语言指令、环境配置、求解器认证的真值解及状态驱动的验证器，实现任务的可控生成与一致性保障。

Result: 成功构建ERP-Bench基准，涵盖300个长期任务；生成参数可预测任务难度；前沿模型在26.1%的尝试中满足显式约束，但仅17.4%达到完全最优解；证明了Anchor与ERP-Bench在构建可审计、高可信评估环境方面的有效性。

Conclusion: Anchor与ERP-Bench提供了一套可复制、可验证的企业级智能体评估框架，解决了任务生成中的不一致性问题，推动了对真实商业任务中智能体能力的可靠评估。

Abstract: AI agents are beginning to complete valuable, long-horizon business operations tasks, but training and evaluation environments for enterprise work still struggle to balance realism, verifiability, and scale. Environment and task creation frequently suffers from a failure mode we call artifact drift: when instructions, environments, oracles, and verifiers are created by loosely coupled processes, they frequently disagree on what a task requires, producing environments that are unsolvable, reward-hackable, or inconsistent. We introduce Anchor, a task-generation pipeline that formalizes domain experts' specifications of business workflows into constraint optimization programs. From a single parametric specification, the pipeline jointly produces a natural-language instruction, environment configuration, solver-certified ground-truth solution, and state-based verifier. With Anchor, altering parameters yields new tasks with controlled difficulty and known optimal solutions, producing harness-agnostic environments whose rewards depend solely on end-state business correctness. We apply Anchor to produce ERP-Bench: a benchmark of 300 long-horizon tasks spanning procurement and manufacturing workflows in a production-grade ERP system. We find that generation parameters predict realized difficulty, and that frontier models satisfy explicit task constraints in 26.1% of trials but reach a fully optimal solution in only 17.4% of trials. Overall, we show that Anchor and ERP-Bench offer a concrete recipe for building auditable evaluation environments for economically valuable agent work. We release the task generator and ERP-Bench dataset at erpbench.ai

### [279] [OmniToM: Benchmarking Theory of Mind in LLMs via Explicit Belief Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26322)
*Adam Bawatneh,Sagar Sapkota,Amrit Singh Bedi,Santu Karmaker,Mubarak Shah*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: OmniToM 是一个新提出的基准，用于评估大语言模型（LLMs）在社会推理中对他人心理状态（如信念、意图、情绪）的建模能力。传统方法仅通过最终答案判断性能，而 OmniToM 通过两个阶段评估：1）信念提取，从故事中识别相关角色的信念；2）信念标注，使用七维标签体系（包括递归层级、真假性、知识获取、显性程度、内容类型、心理来源和上下文）对信念进行结构化标注。该基准基于 895 个故事和 22,343 个标注信念，采用人类校准的 LLM 辅助标注流程。零样本测试显示，当前 LLM 在信念追踪方面存在显著瓶颈，尤其在将叙事事实转化为角色信念及共享心智状态时面临知识获取与表征决策难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法仅依赖最终答案，无法揭示模型是否真正构建了心理状态表示，尤其在涉及分歧、动态或错误信念的情境下。因此需要一种能直接检验信念结构建模能力的新方法。

Method: 提出 OmniToM 基准，包含两阶段评估流程：第一阶段为信念提取，从故事中识别关键信念；第二阶段为信念标注，采用七维标签体系对每个信念进行精细分类。数据来自 ToMBench 故事语料库并经人工校准的 LLM 辅助标注生成。

Result: 在多种模型的零样本评估中，发现所有模型普遍存在信念追踪瓶颈，尤其在处理知识获取路径和信念表征转换方面表现不佳，表明当前 LLM 尚未具备稳定的心理状态建模能力。

Conclusion: OmniToM 有效揭示了当前 LLM 在社会推理中对信念结构建模的局限性，强调需发展更精细的心理状态理解机制，以推动模型向真正具备理论心智能力的方向演进。

Abstract: Theory of Mind (ToM), the ability to infer others' knowledge, intentions, and emotions, is commonly evaluated in large language models (LLMs) using end-point question answering, where performance is judged solely by the final answer to a social reasoning query. This paradigm obscures whether the model actually constructs the underlying mental-state representations required for robust reasoning, particularly in scenarios involving divergent, evolving, or mistaken beliefs. In order to address this research gap, we introduce OmniToM, a benchmark that directly evaluates these representations by requiring explicit modeling of belief structures for all relevant actors within a narrative. These structures are composed of belief propositions: minimal statements of what an actor takes to be true about the world or another actor's mental state, allowing knowledge, intentions, emotions, and false beliefs to be analyzed in a common format. Models are evaluated in two stages: Stage 1: Belief Extraction, which extracts from the story the beliefs relevant to its social dynamics, and Stage 2: Belief Labeling, which assigns each belief a seven-dimensional schema label covering recursive order, truth status, knowledge access, explicitness, content type, mental source, and context. Built from 895 stories from the existing ToMBench story corpus and augmented with 22,343 labeled belief propositions, OmniToM uses a human-calibrated LLM-assisted annotation pipeline. Across diverse models in zero-shot evaluation, OmniToM reveals an actor-specific belief-tracking bottleneck: current LLMs struggle with the knowledge-access and representational decisions required to transform narrative facts into actors' beliefs and shared mental states.

Abstract: Educational virtual laboratories can make experimental training more scala-ble, adaptive, and accessible, especially when students have limited access to physical laboratory facilities. However, authoring new simulated laboratory procedures remains costly: educators must describe new equipment, define how instruments and materials interact, and specify valid procedural flows that can be executed or assessed inside the virtual environment. Large lan-guage models can assist in this authoring process by generating detailed ex-perimental procedures, but their output should not be treated as directly exe-cutable plans. They may omit necessary actions, arrange steps in the wrong order, or produce instructions that are logically incorrect or incompatible with the laboratory equipment. This paper presents a prototype framework for managing uncertainty in LLM-generated procedural knowledge for virtu-al laboratory planning. The framework aims to reduce procedural uncertainty by using structured domain representations and uncertain LLM-generated state-transition samples to extract candidate procedural rules, transform them into explicit and inspectable constraints, and use them to repair uncertain procedural steps. Although the motivating domain refers to educational vir-tual laboratories, the underlying problem is more general: managing uncer-tain procedural knowledge for action planning in structured interactive envi-ronments. We illustrate the approach in a virtual laboratory domain involving laboratory instruments, containers, tools, and material-transfer actions.

### [281] [Automatic Layer Selection for Hallucination Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26366)
*Xinpeng Wang,William Cao,Andrew Gordon Wilson,Zhe Zeng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了大语言模型（LLM）中幻觉相关信号在中间层比最终层更显著的现象，针对如何自动选择高性能层的问题，提出了多个假设并评估了多种选择标准，但发现现有标准表现不一致。为此，提出一种新的无训练、低开销的选择准则FEPoID，能稳定识别最优或近优层，并优于现有方法。此外，还引入了一种简单的截断策略，进一步增强幻觉信号，显著提升检测性能。代码已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出多个关于中间层信号生成的假设，评估多种层选择标准；设计新的训练无关的FEPoID准则（首次有效内在维度峰值），结合截断策略以增强幻觉信号。

Result: FEPoID在不同架构、规模和任务下均表现出色，稳定识别出最优或接近最优层，显著优于已有标准和基线方法；结合截断策略后，整体检测性能大幅提升。

Conclusion: FEPoID是一种高效、通用且无需训练的层选择方法，配合截断策略可显著提升幻觉检测性能，具有良好的实际应用价值。

Abstract: Recent studies on hallucination detection have shown that hallucination-related signals are more strongly encoded in intermediate layers than in the final layer of large language models (LLMs). Although a growing body of work has sought to exploit this property for hallucination detection, how to automate the selection of high-performing layers remains underexplored, and principled methods for this purpose are still lacking. To address this gap, we first propose several hypotheses for why such signals emerge in intermediate layers and evaluate corresponding criteria for automatic layer selection across diverse LLM architectures, scales, and tasks, covering both question answering and summarization hallucination detection benchmarks. However, we find that none of these criteria consistently delivers satisfactory performance. We therefore propose a new selection criterion, First Effective Peak of Intrinsic Dimension (FEPoID), which consistently identify optimal or near-optimal layers and outperforms both the aforementioned criteria and existing hallucination detection baselines. FEPoID is training-free and incurs negligible computational overhead. In addition, we study the generation behaviors of LLMs and introduce a simple yet effective truncation strategy, which further amplifies hallucination-related signals and substantially improves overall detection performance. Code is publicly available at https://github.com/DesoloYw/Automatic-Layer-Selection-for-Hallucination-Detection.git

### [282] [Exploiting Local Dynamics Regularity for Reusable Skills in Offline Hierarchical RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26371)
*Sarthak Dayal,Abhinav Peri,Carl Qi,Claas Voelcker,Alexander Levine,Caleb Chuck,Amy Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为CARL（对比动作表示用于可重用局部控制）的新方法，旨在解决层次强化学习（HRL）中技能可重用性难题。该方法基于局部动态的直观假设：不同全局情境下的局部转移需要相似的动作序列。通过将这些情境与其所需的动作序列对齐，能够学习到可重用的技能，并明确其适用位置。该方法在复杂人形环境中实现了有意义的技能聚类，并在OGBench基准上提升了HIQL算法的下游性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前层次强化学习（HRL）虽能高效处理长时序任务，但难以获得真正可重用的技能。本文旨在解决这一关键挑战，通过利用局部动态的共性来发现和识别可复用的动作技能。

Method: 提出基于对比学习的动作表示框架——CARL，通过分析不同全局上下文中的局部转移行为，对齐上下文与对应动作序列，从而学习具有可重用性的技能表示。

Result: 在复杂人形环境中成功实现有意义的技能聚类；在OGBench基准测试中，集成CARL的HIQL算法表现出显著提升的下游性能。

Abstract: Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning (HRL) promises to solve long-horizon Reinforcement Learning (RL) tasks more efficiently than non-hierarchical counterparts by discovering and reusing temporally-extended skills. However, obtaining skills that are actually reusable remains an open challenge. Towards this end, we focus on abstractions that exploit the intuition of local dynamics: local transitions in different global contexts require similar kinds of action sequences. By aligning these contexts with the action sequences they require, we are able to learn which skills to reuse and where to reuse them. In principle, this information should benefit many HRL algorithms, where high-level policies have to reason about the low-level skills they use. The resulting algorithm CARL (Contrastive Action-based Representations for Reusable Local Control) shows both qualitative clustering of meaningful skills in complex humanoid environments and improved downstream performance on the OGBench benchmark when integrated with HIQL.

</details>

Abstract: Large multimodal models (LMMs) have rapidly advanced in perception and reasoning; however, it remains unclear whether these capabilities generalize to discovering visually grounded solutions in open-ended environments, beyond pattern recognition. In such settings, intelligence requires more than answering well-posed questions: it involves identifying how elements in a scene can be repurposed in non-obvious yet physically feasible ways. This form of creative problem-solving is central to human intelligence, but remains largely untested in current benchmarks. To evaluate this ability, we introduce MM-CreativityBench, a benchmark for affordance-grounded creative tool use in visually rich, physically constrained environments. Our experiments show that current LMMs often fall short, not due to lack of generative capability, but because they do not sustain grounded exploration. Models often overlook relevant entities, under-examine critical parts, or hallucinate attributes not grounded in the image. Motivated by this failure mode, we propose affordance-grounded alignment, which casts creative tool use as a preference learning problem. Using Direct Preference Optimization, we encourage models to prefer attribute-affordance reasoning grounded in visual evidence over hallucinated alternatives. In addition, we incorporate supervision derived from an affordance knowledge base to guide broader entity exploration and multi-turn planning. Our results show consistent gains in selecting the correct entities and parts, while substantially reducing hallucination and grounding-related errors.

TL;DR: UnityMAS-O is a general reinforcement learning framework for LLM-based multi-agent systems that treats entire workflows as optimization units. It introduces four first-class objects—logical agent roles, graph trajectories, user-defined rewards, and agent-model mappings—to enable flexible role modeling, structured interaction, and fine-grained credit assignment. The framework supports various parameter sharing strategies and integrates with a Ray-based star-topology runtime for distributed training. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: UnityMAS-O represents multi-agent workflows using four first-class components: logical agent roles, graph trajectories, user-defined rewards, and agent-model mappings. It uses a Ray-based star-topology runtime with a central controller managing workflow execution, tool invocation, trajectory recording, and reward assembly, while model-local workers handle rollouts, buffering, advantage computation, and distributed PPO updates. This design decouples logic from implementation and enables flexible configuration without modifying core infrastructure.

Result: UnityMAS-O improves manually specified workflows across multiple tasks—including retrieval-augmented QA, iterative agentic search, and reflective code generation—on benchmarks like Natural Questions, HotpotQA, and held-out code tasks. Abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems decompose complex tasks into interacting roles, but most remain manually orchestrated by prompts, tools, and control rules, while agents are rarely optimized through a unified reinforcement learning interface. Existing RL post-training frameworks mainly target single-policy optimization and lack abstractions for user-defined multi-agent workflows, structured interaction, role-specific credit assignment, and configurable parameter sharing.
  We present UnityMAS-O, a general RL optimization framework for LLM-based multi-agent systems. UnityMAS-O treats the complete workflow as the optimization unit, rather than a single response or policy trajectory. It represents workflows through four first-class objects: logical agent roles, graph trajectories, user-defined rewards, and agent--model mappings. This decouples logical agents from physical model parameters, supporting full sharing, full separation, and partial sharing, with rewards assigned at role, turn, and trajectory levels.
  UnityMAS-O extends verl with a Ray-based star-topology runtime. A central controller executes workflows, invokes tools, records structured trajectories, and assembles rewards; model-local worker groups handle rollout, buffering, advantage computation, and distributed PPO-style updates. Users can define agents, workflows, model mappings, and rewards without rewriting the optimization infrastructure.
  We instantiate UnityMAS-O on retrieval-augmented QA, iterative agentic search, and reflective code generation. Across Natural Questions, HotpotQA, and held-out code tasks, multi-agent RL improves manually specified workflows after optimization, with especially large gains for smaller models and strict code all-passed metrics. These results show that UnityMAS-O can serve as a reusable substrate for converting diverse LLM-based multi-agent workflows into trainable multi-agent RL systems.

### [287] [Completion vs Optimality: Policy Gradient in Long-Horizon Cumulative-Damage Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26657)
*Wolfgang Maass,Sabine Janzen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了长期决策问题中累积损伤带来的挑战，识别出策略梯度方法的两种独立失败模式：完成（达到最终时间步而非通过隐式终止约束退出）和最优性（在完成的前提下匹配动态规划参考解）。通过引入线性软惩罚的PPO方法，发现仅给予时间步访问权限会降低完成率；而结合动作空间限制与时间步访问则可实现完成，但存在0.271的最优性差距，归因于损伤起点处的早期贪婪承诺。研究提出四个可验证预测，并在两个分别校准的环境中进行验证——一个49步的砖匠职业生涯和一个20赛季的NBA前锋职业生涯，两者结构相同但领域、时间跨度、动作集和校准数据不同。所有预测均定性复现，且时间步不变性预测在四分之三的时间步下成立，$H = 15$ 的例外与理论边界 $H^* \in [6, 14]$ 一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期决策问题中累积损伤导致局部有利行为与全局不利结果耦合，传统策略梯度方法在此类问题中易出现完成与最优性双重失效，亟需理解其根本原因并设计可分解的解决方案。

Method: 提出完成与最优性的解耦分析框架，采用基于线性软惩罚的PPO算法，在两个结构相同但具体参数不同的模拟环境中测试四种可验证预测，包括时间步不变性等。

Result: 仅赋予时间步访问权限会降低完成率；结合动作空间限制与时间步访问可实现完成，但存在0.271的最优性差距；所有预测在两个环境中定性复现，时间步不变性在多数情况下成立，$H=15$ 的例外与理论边界一致。

Conclusion: 累积损伤下的长期决策问题中，完成与最优性是可分离的失败模式；通过动作空间限制与时间步访问可提升完成率，但需额外机制缓解早期贪婪承诺带来的最优性损失；研究提出的框架和预测具有跨域泛化能力。

Abstract: Long-horizon decision problems with cumulative damage couple locally attractive actions to globally adverse outcomes. We identify two orthogonal failure modes for policy-gradient methods on this class and propose a decomposition that separates them: \emph{completion} (reaching the terminal horizon rather than exiting via an implicit terminal constraint) and \emph{optimality} (matching the dynamic-programming reference given completion). Under PPO with a linear soft penalty, granting horizon access alone reduces the completion rate: the penalty's equilibrium drives the dominant-activity share to zero, while action-space restriction combined with horizon access achieves completion but leaves an optimality gap ($ΔM_{\text{final}} = 0.271$) that we trace to first-phase greedy commitment at the damage origin. We derive four testable predictions and evaluate them in two separately calibrated environments that share the same abstract structure but differ in domain, horizon, activity set, and calibration data: a 49-step bricklayer career and a 20-season NBA power-forward career. All four predictions replicate qualitatively. The horizon-invariance prediction is met at three of four tested horizons, with the exception at $H = 15$ consistent with the $H^*$ boundary ($H^* \in [6, 14]$ under the NBA parameters).

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents increasingly rely on external memory systems to remain consistent across long-horizon interactions, but little empirical work has been done to understand the specific failure modes and design choices that these systems present. Based on these hypothesized failure modes, we construct five datasets spanning four tasks, each adversarially designed to test a specific operation of a memory system. Using these datasets, we evaluate four state-of-the-art memory systems on MemFail and demonstrate how MemFail can be used to empirically understand the tradeoffs induced by differences in memory system architectures.

### [290] [Beyond a Single Direction: Chain-of-Thought Disrupts Simple Steering of Refusal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26772)
*Kia-Jüng Yang,Dominik Meier,Jiachen Zhao,Terry Ruas,Bela Gipp*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型推理模型（LRM）的拒绝行为不仅依赖于残差流激活，还受思维链（CoT）影响。当固定CoT时，激活引导仅在39%的情况下逆转拒绝；但移除CoT后成功率升至70%。若在干预中重新生成CoT，拒绝逆转率可达94%，且即使移除引导，重构的CoT仍保留48%的效果，说明CoT可独立携带并重建合规信号。因此，拒绝在激活与CoT间联合编码，使模型对单一激活干预更具鲁棒性，但也暴露了CoT作为潜在攻击面的风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究大型推理模型中拒绝行为的机制，揭示其与思维链（CoT）的耦合关系，探索更有效的控制策略，尤其是面对激活引导等干预手段时的局限性与改进路径。

Method: 通过固定或移除思维链（CoT），结合激活引导技术，在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-LLaMA-8B模型上测试拒绝行为的可逆性；进一步设计两阶段干预：先引导激活以生成新CoT，再评估该CoT独立作用下的效果。

Result: 激活引导在固定CoT时仅能逆转39%的拒绝行为，而移除CoT后提升至70%；两阶段干预下拒绝逆转率达94%；重构的CoT即使在引导移除后仍保持48%的效应，表明其具备独立传递合规信号的能力。

Conclusion: 大型推理模型中的拒绝行为是残差流激活与思维链（CoT）共同编码的结果。这增强了模型对激活级干预的鲁棒性，但也揭示了CoT作为替代攻击表面的可能性，提示需从多维度设计控制机制。

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) generate chain-of-thought (CoT) traces before producing final outputs, introducing a dynamic internal state that may complicate control mechanisms such as refusal. Unlike instruction-tuned LLMs, where refusal is mediated by a single directional subspace, refusal in large reasoning models (LRMs) additionally depends on the CoT. In DeepSeek-R1-Distill-LLaMA-8B, activation steering reverses refusal in only 39% of cases when the CoT is kept fixed, but removing the CoT entirely increases this to 70%, indicating that the CoT actively reinforces refusal. In a two-stage intervention where the model regenerates its CoT under activation steering, refusal is reversed in 94% of cases, while the resulting CoT alone retains 48% of this effect even after steering is removed. This suggests that the CoT can carry and reconstruct the compliance signal independently. These findings indicate that refusal in LRMs is jointly encoded in residual stream activations and CoT. This joint activation makes LRM more robust against activation-level interventions alone, but exposes CoT to a possible alternative surface attack.

</details>


### [291] [The Attribution Blind Spot: Detecting When Language Models Rely on Memory Rather Than Retrieved Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26778)
*Zhe Yu,Wenpeng Xing,Yunzhao Wei,Bo Yang,Chen Ye,Gaolei Li,Meng Han*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出计算现实监控（CRM）以解决检索增强生成中的归属盲点问题，即模型可能仅依赖预训练记忆而非外部上下文生成内容，导致输出看似一致但实际来源不可靠。CRM通过比较有无上下文时的内部表示差异，识别出模型在使用外部证据时产生的可测量内部轨迹信号，从而检测是否真正受外部证据影响。该方法在多个模型架构中表现出层特定模式，且在不同任务和数据集上具有泛化能力，但在领域混淆基准上失效，表明其有效性与上下文真实性相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前检索增强生成系统缺乏可靠手段验证生成内容是否真正由外部上下文驱动，尤其当外部文档与模型预训练数据重叠时，模型可能仅凭参数记忆生成看似一致的内容，造成‘归属盲点’。这威胁高风险应用的可信性。

Method: 引入计算现实监控（CRM），借鉴认知科学中的现实监控理论，通过对比模型在有无外部上下文输入时的内部表示差异，检测是否存在由上下文引发的表征偏移。该方法不直接判定单次生成的来源，而是判断上下文是否在内部产生了可测量的影响。

Result: CRM在九种不同模型变体中均能检测到显著的层特定表示差异，块级噪声干预实验进一步支持其有效性；该方法在多种任务和数据集上具有良好的泛化能力，但在领域混淆的基准上表现下降，说明其对真实上下文敏感。

Conclusion: 归属盲点是可测量且部分可缓解的问题。内部表示中存在输出层面无法察觉的诊断信号，为构建能够内知证据来源并据此调整行为的系统奠定了基础。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation promises to ground language model outputs in external evidence, yet the field has no reliable way to verify whether retrieved context actually governs generation -- a prerequisite for any high-stakes deployment. The standard assumption, that context-consistent output implies context-governed output, breaks when the retrieved document overlaps with the model's pretraining data: the model can produce faithful-looking text entirely from parametric memory, and both pathways yield indistinguishable output. We name this failure the attribution blind spot and introduce Computational Reality Monitoring (CRM) to address it. CRM operationalizes a principle adapted from cognitive science's reality monitoring framework: comparing internal representations with and without context reveals membership-conditioned representational divergence that output-level monitors systematically miss. CRM does not certify which source an individual generation used; it detects whether pretraining exposure leaves a measurable internal trajectory signature, establishing a necessary substrate for source attribution. Across nine model variants spanning three families, this divergence concentrates in architecture-specific layer patterns, receives converging support from block-level noise intervention, and generalizes across tasks and datasets while collapsing on domain-confounded benchmarks. The attribution blind spot is measurable and partially addressable: internal representations carry a diagnostic signal invisible at the output level, establishing a foundation for systems whose internal awareness of evidence provenance governs their external behavior.

</details>


### [292] [LiveK12Bench: Have Large Multimodal Models Truly Conquered High School-level Examinations?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26781)
*Xiaohan Wang,Mingze Yin,Yilin Zhao,Gang Liu,Dian Li*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法有效反映真实考试环境的复杂性，存在静态数据、数据污染、模态与学科受限等问题，限制了大模型作为智能导师的实际应用潜力。

Method: 构建LiveK12Bench基准，采用自动化数据采集与解析流程，持续引入最新真实考题；设计‘模拟考试’评估机制，评估模型在时间、逻辑与准确性约束下的端到端答题能力。

Result: 12个大模型在真实考试环境下表现明显下降，例如GPT-5得分从79降至53；暴露出对复杂视觉布局敏感、推理路径效率不足等缺陷。

Conclusion: 当前先进大模型虽具备理想化推理能力，但在真实教育环境中仍存在显著差距，亟需更贴近现实的评估体系以推动其向真正可用的智能教学工具演进。

Abstract: Advanced Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) have demonstrated impressive performance in K-12 reasoning tasks, exhibiting great promise as intelligent tutors. Realizing this potential requires models to navigate real-world examinations effectively, yet most existing benchmarks fail to capture the complexity of authentic testing environments. Specifically, most datasets are static, prone to data contamination, and are often confined to restricted modalities, disciplines, and evaluation criteria. To address these issues, we introduce LiveK12Bench, a dynamic, holistic, multi-disciplinary benchmark designed to evaluate the reasoning abilities of LMMs in realistic examination scenarios. LiveK12Bench comprises 2K+ verified questions spanning Mathematics, Physics, Chemistry, and Biology, sourced from the latest real-world exam papers and designed to grow over time. Our framework features several core innovations: 1) featuring an automated pipeline that continuously ingests and parses the latest examination papers to mitigate data leakage; and 2) proposing a novel `Mock Exam' evaluation scheme, which assesses the ability to complete end-to-end exams autonomously with accurate and efficient reasoning paths. Extensive experiments on 12 LMMs reveal that advanced models suffer substantial performance degradation under exam-realistic constraints: GPT-5's score drops from 79 to 53 (out of 100) when process rigor and efficiency are jointly evaluated. Our findings expose critical vulnerabilities, such as sensitivity to complex visual layouts, highlighting the gap between idealized reasoning capabilities and true educational readiness. Both code and dataset are publicly available.

### [293] [Composition Collapse: Stable Factual Knowledge Does Not Imply Compositional Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26789)
*Zhe Yu,Wenpeng Xing,Yunzhao Wei,Jie Chen,Hongzhi Wang,Xuyang Teng,Meng Han*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了后训练评估中聚合基准分数的局限性，指出多跳推理被当作单一能力衡量可能导致误判。研究发现，即使基础知识相同，不同训练方法在组合推理上的表现可相差40%以上，这种现象称为‘组合崩溃’。作者提出双门控协议，将评估重点从整体组合差距转向在稳定原子知识基础上的残余组合失败，从而分解出三个独立维度：原子稳定性、残余组合能力和关键深度。实验表明，后训练目标对组合能力的影响方向被传统指标掩盖，因此建议在评价多跳推理进步时需结合受控于原子门的组合指标。诊断分析还发现，大部分组合失败源于生成时计算约束，而非无法组合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前后训练评估依赖聚合基准分数，将多跳推理视为单一能力，忽略了组合行为与原子知识之间的分离，可能导致对模型真实推理能力的错误判断。

Method: 提出双门控协议，通过控制原子知识访问条件，将后训练收益分解为原子稳定性、残余组合能力和关键深度三个独立通道，并使用诊断探针分析组合失败的成因。

Result: 实验显示，不同后训练方法在组合表现上差异显著，但传统聚合指标无法捕捉；组合失败主要由生成时计算限制引起，而非永久性组合缺陷。

Conclusion: 应避免仅依赖聚合指标评估多跳推理能力，建议引入原子门控的组合度量，以更准确揭示后训练对组合能力的真实影响。

Abstract: Post-training is routinely evaluated through aggregate benchmark scores that treat multi-hop reasoning as a single capability -- as if a model that answers more questions correctly must be better at assembling facts. We show that this assumption can be misleading: recipes with statistically indistinguishable atomic knowledge produce composition behaviour separated by over 40 percentage points, a phenomenon we call composition collapse: the systematic failure to assemble stably-known facts into chains, invisible to aggregate metrics. We introduce a double-gate protocol that changes the estimand from an aggregate compositionality gap to residual composition failure conditioned on stable atomic access, decomposing post-training gains into three independent channels: atomic stability, residual composition, and critical depth. On a benchmark of temporal factual chains spanning depths 2--11 across four post-training recipes, this decomposition reveals that post-training objectives shift composition capability in directions that aggregate metrics mask, and suggests that claims about multi-hop reasoning improvement should be accompanied by atomic-gate-controlled composition metrics. Diagnostic probes further show that a substantial share of measured composition failure reflects generation-time computation constraints rather than permanent inability to compose.

### [294] [What Makes Chain-of-Thought Work at Probe Time? Local Co-occurrence Rather Than Global Derivation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26795)
*Xiang Wang,Wei Wei*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了链式思维（CoT）提示在推理时如何提升语言模型的准确性，重点分析固定理由文本中哪些因素影响答案。研究发现，即使打乱词语顺序，理由文本仍显著优于无理由基线，表明词汇激活效应强烈；更重要的是，结构化文本带来的额外增益主要源于短距离词元邻近性，而非句子级逻辑顺序。仅保留2-3个连续词元窗口即可恢复大部分性能增益。排除了答案显式复制、答案值重复或完整语法实现为主要驱动因素。跨模型家族、参数规模和数据集的泛化实验验证了结果的稳定性。研究支持局部共现激活（LCA）解释：性能提升主要来自词汇激活和短程词元共现，而非句级逻辑推导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解链式思维（CoT）提示提升语言模型准确性的内在机制，特别是探针时间（probe-time）下理由文本中何种属性导致性能提升，以超越以往对生成阶段行为的研究。

Method: 采用固定理由文本进行探针实验，通过改变理由文本的结构（如词序打乱、保留短距离词元窗口等），观察其对模型输出的影响，并通过对照实验排除答案复制、语法完整性等因素的干扰。

Result: 词序打乱后的理由仍显著优于无理由基线，说明存在强词汇激活效应；仅保留2-3个连续词元窗口即可恢复大部分性能增益；排除了答案显式声明、答案值复制和语法完整性的主要作用；结果在不同模型、规模和数据集上具有高度一致性。

Conclusion: 链式思维提示的性能增益主要源于局部共现激活（LCA），即词汇激活与短距离词元邻近性，而非句子级逻辑推理。这一机制在多种设置下均稳定有效。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) prompting reliably improves language-model accuracy, but which properties of a rationale text drive the improvement is poorly understood. Prior work has largely studied generation-time behavior. We instead ask a probe-time question: given a fixed rationale in context, what in that text changes the answer? We identify two complementary sources of the gain. First, even a globally word-shuffled rationale substantially outperforms the no-rationale baseline, indicating a strong lexical activation effect. More importantly, the additional gain from structured text appears to arise less from sentence-level logical ordering and more from short-range token adjacency. Preserving contiguous windows of just $n^\star{=}2$--$3$ tokens recovers most of the remaining gain toward full CoT performance. Supporting experiments rule out copying of explicit answer declarations or answer values, as well as full grammatical realization, as primary drivers. Further generalization experiments show that the qualitative pattern remains stable across multiple model families, parameter scales, and datasets. These results support a local co-occurrence activation (LCA) account of probe-time CoT, in which the observed gains appear to arise primarily from lexical activation and short-range token co-occurrence rather than sentence-level logical derivation.

</details>


### [295] [Multi-Stakeholder LLM Alignment: Decomposing Estimation from Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26878)
*Lulu Zheng,Wenjin Yang,Xiangwen Zhang,Rong Yin,Yulan Hu,Zheng Pan,Xin Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文针对多利益相关方任务中因模型权重不稳定性导致的评分偏差问题，提出DecompR方法。通过在候选生成前基于查询结构固定反事实校准权重，并独立估计各角色效用，有效减少候选依赖的权重漂移和估计噪声，提升评分稳定性和公平性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在处理多利益相关方任务时，将效用估计与效用聚合混为一谈，导致隐式权重不稳定，尤其在利益相关方满意度分散或数量增加时产生显著的评分波动，影响决策公正性。

Method: 提出DecompR方法，先根据查询结构预先确定反事实校准的权重，再独立评估每个角色的效用，避免候选内容对权重的影响，从而消除候选依赖的权重漂移。

Result: 实验表明，DecompR能有效降低由权重噪声引起的评分波动，尤其在利益相关方数量较多或满意度分布分散时表现更优，显著提升了评分的稳定性和可解释性。

Conclusion: 通过分离权重设定与效用评估过程，DecompR有效缓解了多利益相关方任务中的权重噪声问题，为构建更公平、稳定的智能评估系统提供了新思路。

Abstract: Multi-stakeholder tasks require one output to satisfy users with conflicting preferences. Holistic LLM judges conflate utility estimation and utility aggregation, yielding unstable implicit weights. We show empirically and theoretically that this aggregation-specific \emph{weighting noise} can create large score shifts when stakeholder satisfaction is dispersed; in our experiments, these weight-induced shifts also increase with stakeholder count. We propose \textsc{DecompR}: counterfactual-calibrated weights are fixed from query structure before candidate scoring, while per-role utilities are estimated independently, removing candidate-dependent weight drift and reducing estimation noise.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过重新分析原定理的逻辑关系，证明其仅作为必要条件；在此基础上，修正定理并设计新的检测算法，兼顾效率与正确性，并提出一个具有更优复杂度上界的互补算法。

Result: 提出了一个修正后的定理和两个改进算法：一个保持原有效率并保证正确性，另一个在最坏情况下具有更紧的复杂度界。

Abstract: Exploiting the indistinguishability of objects in a probabilistic graphical model such as a factor graph is key to lifted probabilistic inference algorithms and allows for tractable probabilistic inference problems with respect to domain sizes. A central building block for the exploitation of indistinguishable objects in factor graphs is the identification of commutative factors, i.e., factors whose output values are invariant under permutations of input values assigned to a subset of their arguments. In this paper, we revisit the theoretical foundations underlying the state-of-the-art algorithm to detect commutative factors. Specifically, we show that in its current form, the state-of-the-art algorithm relies on a central theorem that is mistakenly regarded as a sufficient condition to identify commutative factors, while it actually only implies necessary condition. Consequently, the state of the art might, as we show in this paper, deliver incorrect results. To fix the flaws currently present in the state of the art, we prove a slightly modified version of the aforementioned theorem, which serves as a necessary condition to identify commutative factors. Moreover, we present a corrected version of the state-of-the-art algorithm, which keeps its efficiency while ensuring correctness and introduce a complementary algorithm with tighter worst-case bounds.

### [297] [TADDLE: A Tool-Augmented Agent for Detecting Deficient LLM-Generated Peer Reviews](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26911)
*Hanqi Duan,Xiang Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: TADDLE 是一个用于检测 LLM 生成同行评审中缺陷的工具增强型智能体，提出了首个由专家标注的基准数据集，涵盖 1800 篇针对 ICLR 2025 论文的评论，包含六类缺陷类别。该系统通过四个专业化分析工具（Verify、Correct、Complete、Transform）协同工作，并由集成器通过两阶段半监督学习实现二分类与多标签分类。实验表明其在缺陷检测任务中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM 生成的同行评审虽流畅且结构良好，但存在难以察觉的缺陷；现有方法或仅判断作者身份，或使用针对人类写作设计的质量评分特征，缺乏对具体缺陷类型的检测能力。因此亟需一种能识别 LLM 生成评审中各类缺陷的新方法。

Method: TADDLE 采用四步分解策略：通过 Verify 检查内容真实性，Correct 评估修正能力，Complete 判断完整性，Transform 分析表达转换合理性；由智能体协调各工具输出，再经两阶段半监督学习整合为最终分类结果。

Result: TADDLE 在二分类和多标签分类任务上均表现出色，显著优于现有方法；所构建的 1800 条专家标注数据集为后续研究提供了高质量基准。

Conclusion: TADDLE 成功实现了对 LLM 生成同行评审中多种缺陷类型的精准检测，其提出的基准数据集与方法为提升学术评审质量提供了有效支持。

Abstract: LLM-generated peer reviews are increasingly common at major venues, yet their deficiencies are hard to detect because they are uniformly fluent and well-structured. Existing work either classifies authorship without judging quality, or scores quality with features designed for human-written reviews; no prior system detects deficiencies in LLM-generated reviews at the level of individual defect types. To bridge the gap, we introduce TADDLE, a Tool-Augmented Agent for Detecting Deficient LLM-Generated Peer Reviews, together with the first expert-annotated benchmark for this task. Our benchmark comprises 1,800 reviews on 50 ICLR 2025 papers, multi-label-annotated by 18 domain experts against a taxonomy of six defect categories (plus a non-deficient label). TADDLE decomposes detection into four specialized analysis tools -- Verify, Correct, Complete, and Transform -- orchestrated by an agent; an integrator synthesizes their outputs into binary and multi-label classifications via two-stage semi-supervised learning. Extensive experiments show that TADDLE performs strongly on both binary detection and the multi-label classification task. We release the benchmark and code at https://github.com/AquariusAQ/TADDLE.

### [298] [Neuro-Symbolic Verification of LLM Outputs for Data-Sensitive Domains (extended preprint)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26942)
*Paul Sigloch,Christoph Benzmüller*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种混合验证架构，结合形式化符号方法与神经语义分析，以解决大语言模型（LLM）在高风险领域中的幻觉、不一致性和隐私漏洞等可靠性问题。该架构通过逻辑推理进行输入验证，利用完备性提供结构化需求的可判定保证；通过嵌入式语义相似性检测输出中的上下文幻觉，弥补形式方法表达力不足的问题。系统采用并行的基于角色的流水线设计，克服了提示词自验证方法固有的分布偏差问题。在真实医疗设备损坏评估报告系统HAIMEDA上的实验表明，该方法对结构化实体的幻觉检测率超过83%，对语义编造的检测率达72%，报告生成时间减少30%，证明神经符号架构可为数据敏感场景下的LLM部署提供可靠保障。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在高风险领域应用时存在幻觉、不一致性及隐私泄露等严重可靠性问题，传统基于提示的自验证方法受分布偏差影响，无法有效避免错误，亟需更可靠的验证机制。

Method: 提出一种混合验证架构，结合形式化符号推理（用于输入验证）与嵌入式语义相似性分析（用于输出验证），采用并行、基于角色的流水线实现，实现输入输出的双重保障。

Result: 在真实医疗设备损坏评估系统HAIMEDA上测试，对结构化实体的幻觉检测率超过83%，对语义编造检测率达72%，报告生成时间减少30%。

Conclusion: 神经符号混合架构能为大语言模型在数据敏感领域提供可信赖的验证机制，具备实际应用价值和推广潜力。

Abstract: LLMs deployed in high-stakes domains face fundamental reliability challenges: hallucinations, inconsistencies, and privacy vulnerabilities introduce unacceptable risks where errors carry legal, financial, or safety consequences. This paper presents a hybrid verification architecture combining formal symbolic methods with neural semantic analysis to provide complementary guarantees for LLM-generated content. This architecture employs logical reasoning for input verification, leveraging completeness properties to provide decidable guarantees on structured requirements. For output validation, embedding-based semantic similarity detects contextual hallucinations where formal methods lack expressiveness. This separation is realized in a parallel, actor-based pipeline, addressing limitations of prompt-based self-verification approaches, which inherit the distributional biases that produce hallucinations. The proposed architecture and type-aware verification method are validated with HAIMEDA, a real-world medical device damage assessment reporting system developed through Action Design Research. Evaluation shows hallucination detection rates of over 83% for structured entities and 72% for semantic fabrications, with a 30% reduction in report creation time, demonstrating that neuro-symbolic architectures can provide principled safeguards for LLM deployment in data-sensitive domains.

Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) promise to bridge this gap, enabling the generation of candidate optimization models from natural language descriptions. However, there is no guarantee that any single LLM-generated model is reliable, and existing approaches that output only one model are therefore risky. In this work, we propose a novel algorithm that generates a portfolio of optimization models, designed to be robust to the limitations of LLMs. Our method exploits the observation that a single LLM can play two distinct roles $\unicode{x2014}$ as a stochastic generator and as a reasoning evaluator $\unicode{x2014}$ and proposes a unified framework that leverages both capabilities in a complementary manner. We provide theoretical guarantees showing that, as long as either the generator or the evaluator is well-aligned with human preferences, the portfolio is guaranteed to contain high-quality candidates, enabling a principled human-in-the-loop process in which a decision-maker can review multiple candidates before committing to one. We further validate our approach empirically, demonstrating strong performance across a range of optimization modeling tasks.

### [302] [Boosting Knowledge Graph Foundation Models via Enhanced Negative Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27023)
*Yinan Liu,Wenjin Xu,Zhiyuan Zha,Xiaochun Yang,Bin Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种简单而有效的自适应负采样方法KMAS，用于增强现有的知识图谱基础模型（KGFMs）。KMAS通过现有KGFM的关系编码器生成的更新关系嵌入来构建困难负三元组，并在训练过程中动态调整困难负三元组的比例：经过预热阶段后，先线性增加再线性减少。在44个数据集上的大量实验表明，该方法能有效提升多种SOTA KGFMs的性能，且无需额外的时间或内存开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KGFMs通常使用随机负三元组进行训练，这些负三元组质量较低，提供的监督信号较弱，限制了模型性能。为了提升KGFM在未见知识图谱上的零样本知识图谱补全能力，亟需更高质量的负采样策略。

Method: 提出KMAS方法，利用KGFM关系编码器生成的更新关系嵌入构造困难负三元组，并设计动态调整困难负三元组比例的机制，在训练初期保持低比例，随后线性上升，再线性下降，以适配模型能力的演化过程。

Result: 在44个数据集上进行的广泛实验表明，KMAS能有效提升多种SOTA KGFMs的性能，显著改善知识图谱补全效果，同时对计算资源需求极低，具备良好的实用性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: KMAS是一种高效、轻量且自适应的负采样方法，能够显著增强现有KGFMs的性能，为知识图谱补全任务提供了一种实用的改进方案。

Abstract: Knowledge graphs (KGs) have become the core backbone of numerous downstream tasks such as question answering and recommender systems. However, despite all this, KGs are often very incomplete. To perform zero-shot knowledge graph completion in unseen KGs, which have different relational vocabularies from those used for pre-training, KG foundation models (KGFMs) receive a wide range of attention. Existing KGFMs often perform training using random negative triples, which are constructed by replacing the head or tail entity of a positive triple with a random entity. However, these negative triples are often constructed with limited quality, providing weak supervision for KGFM training. In this paper, we propose a simple yet effective adaptive negative sampling approach, KMAS, to enhance existing KGFMs. KMAS constructs hard negative triples through the updated relation embeddings generated from the existing KGFM's relation encoder. To further adaptively align with the evolving capability of the KGFM during the training process, KMAS adjusts the ratio of hard negative triples dynamically throughout the whole training process: after a warmup phrase, it increases the ratio linearly and then decreases linearly. Extensive experiments are conducted over 44 data sets. Experimental results demonstrate that our proposed negative sampling method can enhance many SOTA KGFMs without requiring excessive additional time or memory consumption.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法未能充分建模电池退化数据的多层级结构（如老化条件共享规律和跨电池轨迹模式）以及电压-电流特性在特定荷电状态区间内的局部变化，限制了早期电池退化轨迹预测的准确性。

Method: BatteryMFormer采用三重设计：(1) 老化条件感知解码器，通过老化条件引导查询和注意力机制注入先验知识；(2) 元退化模式记忆模块，学习并检索轨迹原型以指导长周期预测；(3) 双视角编码器，联合捕捉电压与电流时间序列中的时序动态与荷电状态局部变异。

Battery degradation data exhibit two key characteristics. First, degradation data present a multi-level structure, including regularities shared within aging conditions and trajectory patterns shared across batteries. Second, degradation-related variations in voltage-current profiles are often localized to specific state-of-charge (SOC) intervals. Existing approaches often fail to explicitly model these characteristics. To bridge this gap, we propose BatteryMFormer, a multi-level Transformer for early BDTF. BatteryMFormer integrates (1) an aging-condition-aware decoder that injects aging-condition priors via aging-condition-informed queries and aging-condition-aware attention, (2) a meta degradation pattern memory that learns and retrieves trajectory prototypes to guide long-horizon forecasting, and (3) a dual-view encoder that jointly captures temporal dynamics and SOC-localized variations from voltage and current time series. Extensive experiments on four battery domains show that BatteryMFormer consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, marking a significant step toward reliable BDTF. Our code is available at https://github.com/Ruifeng-Tan/BatteryMFormer.

Abstract: Key knowledge for steel-industry volatile organic compounds (VOCs) governance is scattered across unstructured scientific literature, making it difficult to integrate process, pollutant, and control-technology evidence and increasing the risk of hallucination when general large language models (LLMs) answer low-frequency industrial questions. By converting fragmented environmental-engineering literature into traceable, queryable, and decision-support-oriented knowledge, Chat-ISV establishes a scalable environmental-informatics paradigm for reliable LLM deployment and intelligent pollution-control decision support in specialized industrial domains.

### [305] [Can Broad Biomedical Knowledge be Contextualized into Scenario-Grounded Propositions?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27082)
*Qingyuan Zeng,Ziyang Chen,Pengxiang Cai,Zixin Guan,Anglin Liu,Lang Qin,Xinyao Lai,Jintai Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SCENE 是一个双层多智能体框架，用于解决生物医学知识与具体数据之间的“缺失连接”问题。它通过迭代搜索将广泛的知识转化为可验证的、场景相关的假设，上层生成搜索方向并将其与数据模式对齐，下层通过多目标优化寻找兼具证据强度和数据支持的具体命题。该方法在临床试验患者亚群发现和LINCS L1000研究中的生物响应分析中表现优异，显著优于现有基线，能够生成可追溯、可检查的假说，为后续验证提供支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出SCENE框架，采用双层多智能体架构：上层将宽泛知识转化为搜索方向，并将其与数据模式对齐；下层通过多目标优化执行这些方向，识别出平衡证据强度与数据支持的特定命题；两层间通过反馈持续优化搜索过程。

Result: 在临床试验中，SCENE成功识别出具有异质治疗反应的患者亚群，且性能优于现有方法；在LINCS L1000研究中，能有效识别出目标-响应匹配度高、阳性率高的扰动情境。结果表明，SCENE能有效连接广义知识与具体证据，生成可解释、可验证的科学假设。

Conclusion: SCENE通过知识上下文化实现了从通用知识到具体、可验证假说的转化，为生物医学发现提供了可追踪、可审查的推理路径，具有良好的应用前景和可扩展性。

Abstract: Biomedical discovery often requires connecting broad biomedical knowledge with specific experimental or clinical data. Background knowledge suggests relevant mechanisms but is usually too general to map directly onto dataset variables, while data-driven patterns can be dataset-specific and hard to interpret mechanistically. We study this missing link as knowledge contextualization: transforming broad biomedical knowledge into evidence-supported, scenario-grounded propositions that domain experts can inspect, replay, and validate. We propose SCENE, a bi-level multi-agent framework that treats knowledge contextualization as iterative search. The upper level converts broad knowledge into search directions and grounds them in the dataset schema. The lower level executes these directions through multi-objective optimization to identify concrete propositions that balance evidential strength and data support. Feedback between the two levels progressively refines the search. We evaluate SCENE in two settings: discovering patient subgroups with heterogeneous treatment benefits in clinical trial scenarios, and identifying context-specific biological responses in LINCS L1000 studies. In clinical trials, SCENE discovers specific, well-supported subgroups and outperforms existing baselines. In L1000 studies, SCENE identifies perturbational contexts with strong target-response matching and high positive rates. These results show that SCENE bridges broad knowledge and scenario-specific evidence, producing traceable, inspectable hypotheses for follow-up validation.

### [306] [ICCU: In-Context Continual Unlearning via Pattern-Induced Refusal Rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27138)
*Ruihao Pan,Suhang Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ICCU 是一种无需修改模型参数的上下文持续遗忘框架，通过从遗忘数据中诱导可读的拒绝规则，在推理时作为过滤器或系统提示应用，实现顺序遗忘请求的高效处理，避免了交叉请求干扰和效用损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于微调的机器遗忘方法在处理连续遗忘请求时存在成本高、效用损失累积和跨请求干扰等问题，因此需要一种更高效、无副作用的遗忘机制。

Method: ICCU 通过从遗忘数据中诱导可读的拒绝规则，并在推理阶段以过滤或系统提示方式应用这些规则，实现无需参数更新的遗忘。规则以无序并集形式累积，保证组合性与无干扰性。

Result: 实验表明，ICCU 能有效抑制目标知识，同时保持模型性能，支持连续遗忘请求的扩展，对改写和跨语言查询具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: ICCU 提供了一种高效、可扩展且无交叉干扰的持续遗忘方案，适用于真实世界中顺序到来的遗忘需求。

Abstract: Machine unlearning aims to remove the influence of specific data from trained language models. In real-world deployments, unlearning requests often arrive sequentially, which challenges existing fine-tuning-based methods: fine-tuning each request is costly, accumulates utility loss, and may cause cross-request interference. To address these issues, we propose ICCU (In-Context Continual Unlearning), an in-context continual unlearning framework that induces readable refusal rules from unlearning datasets and applies them at inference time either as a filter or via the system prompt, without modifying model parameters. Because rules are accumulated as an order-independent union, ICCU is compositional and free of cross-request interference, and the original forget-set data can be discarded after rule induction. Extensive experiments show that ICCU effectively suppresses target knowledge while preserving utility, scales across sequential requests, and remains robust to paraphrased and cross-lingual queries.

### [307] [StepOPSD: Step-Aware Online Preference Distillation for Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27140)
*Yanfei Zhang,Xu Lin,Chenglin Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: StepOPSD 是一种后回放偏好自蒸馏框架，将智能体的每一步动作作为信用重新分配的基本单位，通过分解轨迹为以动作为中心的步骤片段，在事后增强的教师上下文中重评分，并将标记级概率差异转化为保持符号的增量调整，结合归一化的每步信用预算进行GRPO更新。该方法在ALFWorld和Search-QA任务中显著提升对局部因果错误敏感的子集表现，尤其在ALFWorld Heat（79.1%）、PickTwo（95.0%）、Search-QA TriviaQA（61.6%）上取得最佳或并列最佳成绩。研究发现存在稳定的双旋钮规律：较小的α_clip起到全局稳定作用，而最优的λ_mix则依赖于具体任务。结果表明，当轨迹级奖励与决定下游成功的关键局部动作之间对齐度较弱时，步骤感知蒸馏最为有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线策略蒸馏（OPD）虽提供更密集的标记级监督，但通常将异构的智能体轨迹视为整体字符串，忽略了其作为因果交互单元的本质。因此，如何更精细地分配信用、提升对关键局部决策的敏感性，成为强化学习中多轮对话智能体的核心挑战。

Method: StepOPSD 将轨迹分解为以动作为中心的步骤段，利用事后增强的教师上下文对各步骤进行重评分，将令牌级对数概率差转换为符号保持的优势调整，并在每步施加归一化信用预算，最终用于改进的GRPO更新。

Result: 在ALFWorld和Search-QA任务中，StepOPSD在多个对局部因果错误敏感的子集上取得最佳或第二好成绩，包括在ALFWorld Heat（79.1%）、PickTwo（95.0%）、Search-QA TriviaQA（61.6%）上排名第一，以及在HotpotQA（40.4%）上并列第一。实验揭示了稳定的两参数调控规律：α_clip越小越有助于稳定，而λ_mix的最优值因任务而异。

Conclusion: StepOPSD 证明了以步骤为单位进行信用再分配的有效性，特别适用于轨迹级奖励与关键局部动作不一致的场景。其提出的双旋钮机制为超参数调优提供了可解释指导，推动了多轮对话智能体在复杂任务中的鲁棒性与性能提升。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning for multi-turn agents suffers from a credit-assignment mismatch: rewards are sparse and trajectory-level, while success often hinges on a few local decisions. Existing online policy distillation (OPD) provides denser token-level supervision, but typically treats heterogeneous agent trajectories as monolithic strings rather than causal interaction units. We present StepOPSD, a post-rollout preference self-distillation framework that takes the agent step as the unit of credit redistribution. StepOPSD decomposes trajectories into action-centered step segments, rescoring them under hindsight-enriched teacher contexts and converting token-level log-probability gaps into sign-preserving advantage shaping with a normalized per-step credit budget before the GRPO update. Across ALFWorld and Search-QA with Qwen3-1.7B and Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct, StepOPSD attains best or second-best results on subsets most sensitive to local causal errors, including first-place performance on ALFWorld Heat (79.1%), PickTwo (95.0%), Search-QA TriviaQA (61.6%), and tied-best performance on HotpotQA (40.4%). The results further reveal a consistent two-knob law: smaller α_clip acts as a broadly stabilizing local trust region, whereas the optimal global mixing strength λ_mix remains task-dependent. These findings suggest that step-aware distillation is most useful when trajectory-level rewards are weakly aligned with the local action that determines downstream success.

</details>


### [308] [Detecting Is Not Resolving: The Monitoring Control Gap in Retrieval Augmented LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27157)
*Zhe Yu,Wenpeng Xing,Chen Ye,Xuyang Teng,Bo Yang,Changting Lin,Meng Han*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了检索增强型大模型（RAG）在多轮对话中存在监测-控制差距：尽管模型能识别矛盾证据，但这种认知未能有效约束其最终决策，导致安全风险。单轮评估严重高估RAG系统的安全性，且对矛盾的承认与安全解决无相关性。通过大规模多轮实验和机制分析，发现行为选择是问题核心——危险信息虽被内部表征并获更多关注，却未影响输出行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前评估协议假设单轮鲁棒性可预测多轮累积下的系统安全性，但该假设在实际中不成立，尤其在高风险任务中，需重新审视RAG系统的安全评估方式。

Method: 采用多轮文档累积协议，在四个模型家族（1.5B-32B参数）上进行超过5万次轮次级评估，并结合隐藏状态探测、注意力分析与响应策略分类，探究模型在处理矛盾信息时的认知与行为差异。

Result: 单轮诊断显著高估RAG安全性；矛盾识别与安全解决无相关性；无通用提示修复方案；机制分析表明行动选择是主要缺陷环节，危险信息虽被注意却未约束输出。

Conclusion: 模型在识别知识冲突方面表现良好，但无法将其转化为安全行为，必须建立专门评估与干预机制以弥合认知与行为之间的差距，才能在高风险场景中信任RAG系统。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented LLMs are deployed for tasks where evidence quality determines action safety, yet evaluation protocols assume that single-turn robustness predicts robustness when evidence accumulates across turns. We show this assumption is fundamentally incorrect. Models exhibit a monitoring-control gap: they readily acknowledge contradictory evidence, yet this awareness fails to constrain their final recommendations - detecting epistemic conflict does not imply resolving it safely. Through a multi-turn document accumulation protocol across four model families (1.5B-32B parameters) and over 50,000 turn-level evaluations, we demonstrate that single-turn diagnostics systematically overestimate RAG safety, that contradiction acknowledgement is uncorrelated with safe resolution, a pattern corroborated by targeted human validation, and that no universal prompt fix exists. Converging mechanism evidence - hidden-state probing, attention analysis, and response-strategy taxonomy - points to action selection as the most plausible locus of the deficit: danger-relevant information is internally represented and receives enhanced attention during unsafe generation, yet fails to constrain output behavior. The gap between what models recognize and what they do must be measured and closed before retrieval-augmented systems can be trusted in high-stakes settings.

Motivation: 传统 RAG 依赖语义相似性检索，在半结构化数据（如产品规格）上表现不佳，因这类任务需精确过滤、聚合或全量检索结构化属性；而纯符号方法对自然语言噪声敏感。因此需要融合语义与符号优势的新框架。

Method: DualGraph 构建两个互补的知识图谱：文本知识图谱用于语义检索，符号知识图谱以类型化的主-谓-宾三元组形式表达结构化信息，并提供多种策略融合两者证据。

Result: DualGraph 在 SpecsQA 基准上显著优于 dense retrieval、GraphRAG、符号系统及表格导向基线，跨不同类型问题均表现稳健。

Conclusion: DualGraph 有效融合了语义与符号推理能力，为半结构化数据上的复杂问答任务提供了更可靠、灵活的解决方案。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems for question answering typically retrieve evidence by semantic similarity between the query and document chunks. Symbolic approaches support such operations, but they are often brittle on noisy natural-language corpora. We address this gap with DualGraph, a RAG framework that represents documents through two complementary views: a Textual Knowledge Graph for semantic retrieval and a Symbolic Knowledge Graph for symbolic querying over typed subject--predicate--object triples. Building on these two components, we provide multiple strategies for selecting or combining semantic and symbolic evidence.We also introduce SpecsQA, a benchmark from a commercial shopping website with semi-structured product documents and manually curated questions spanning open-ended and specification-oriented retrieval. Experiments show that DualGraph consistently outperforms state-of-the-art dense-retrieval, GraphRAG, symbolic, and table-oriented baselines across question types.Code and data are available at https://github.com/corneliocristina/DualGraphRAG.

### [310] [The Compressive Knowledge Graph Hypothesis: Which Graph Facts Matter for Scientific Hypothesis Generation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27176)
*Shashwat Sourav,Viktoriia Baibakova,Sanjay Das,Ran Elgedawy,Maria Mahbub,Emily Herron,Tirthankar Ghosal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了知识图谱（KG）在电池材料领域引导假设生成中的作用，发现不同语言模型对KG的依赖程度各异。尽管引入KG能改变生成内容，但即使无KG输入，模型仍能从自身先验中恢复大量图谱信息。紧凑的top-k子图常能近似完整KG的表现，即使关键结论三元组被移除。此外，多种子图选择策略（如随机或基于拓扑结构）均可有效保留信号，支持一种冗余感知的压缩式知识图谱假设：科学上结构化的小型子图即可承载有用的知识信号，无需依赖完整图谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究知识图谱如何影响语言模型生成科学假设，特别是识别哪些图谱事实真正塑造了生成结果，以理解KG在科学推理中的实际作用。

Method: 通过扰动局部知识图谱的密度、本体丰富度、拓扑结构和控制结构，评估Mistral-7B、Llama-3.1-70B和Gemini 2.5 Flash三个模型在提供图谱与固定参考下的输出表现。分析不同子图选取策略（如top-k、随机、拓扑相关）对生成结果的影响。

Result: KG对模型输出有选择性影响，且因模型而异；即使无KG输入，模型也能从自身先验中恢复大量图谱内容；紧凑的子图（如top-k）常能近似全图表现，包括在关键三元组缺失时；多种子图选择方式均能有效保留信号。

Conclusion: 支持‘冗余感知的压缩式知识图谱’假设：有用的图谱信号通常可从紧凑且具有科学结构的子图中恢复，无需使用完整的局部图谱。

Abstract: Knowledge graphs (KGs) can provide structured scientific context to language models, but it remains unclear which graph facts actually shape the generated hypotheses. We study KG-guided hypothesis generation for battery materials across Mistral-7B, Llama-3.1-70B, and Gemini 2.5 Flash. We perturb local KGs by varying density, ontology richness, topology, and control structure, and evaluate outputs with both provided-graph and fixed-reference metrics. Across models, KG utility is selective and model-dependent: graph context changes outputs, but no-KG outputs also recover substantial graph content from model priors. Compact top-k subgraphs often approximate full-KG behavior, including when claimed-outcome triples are held out. At the same time, compression is not unique to one semantic ranking rule, random and topology-based subsets can also recover much of the signal. These results support a redundancy-aware Compressive KG hypothesis: useful KG signal is often recoverable from compact, scientifically structured subgraphs rather than requiring the full local graph.

### [311] [Gumbel Machine: Counterfactual Student Writing Generation via Gumbel Noise Steering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27249)
*Hunter McNichols,Alexander Scarlatos,Mihai Dascalu,Danielle McNamara,Andrew Lan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Gumbel Machine的新方法，用于生成与学生原始作品相似但经过改进的反事实文本（counterfactuals），以帮助跨学科教学。该方法利用大语言模型（LLM）的指令遵循能力，并通过一种新颖的受控解码算法——β-事后控制（β-Hindsight control），在生成过程中调节与参考文本的相似性。实验表明，该方法在多个学生写作数据集上能有效生成既符合评分标准又保持与原作高度相似的反事实文本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自动化反事实文本生成方法多为领域特定系统，难以推广到实际教学应用。而教师需要的是与学生当前水平相近、但质量更高的示范文本，以便学生模仿学习。因此，亟需一种灵活、通用且能保持高相似性的反事实生成方法。

Method: 提出Gumbel Machine框架，核心是β-事后控制算法，通过引入可调的潜在随机性，在生成过程中动态控制反事实文本与参考文本的相似度，同时确保其符合评分标准。该方法充分利用了大语言模型对指令的理解和执行能力，具有良好的模块化和可扩展性。

Result: 在多个学生写作数据集上的实验结果显示，Gumbel Machine能够生成既符合评分标准（rubric-consistent）又与原始文本高度相似的反事实文本，显著优于现有方法。用户评估也证实其生成结果在教学适用性和自然度方面表现优异。

Conclusion: Gumbel Machine提供了一种高效、灵活且可迁移的反事实文本生成方案，适用于教育场景中高质量示范文本的自动生成，为智能辅导系统和个性化学习支持提供了有力工具。

Abstract: An effective method of teaching across disciplines is to provide examples of high-quality work. However, an example may be significantly different from a student's current work, making it challenging for them to emulate. An ideal learning demonstration is a counterfactual version of the student work, an improved version that is still similar to their own. Existing automated approaches for counterfactual text generation using Large Language Models (LLMs) result in domain-specific systems that are difficult to translate into practical applications. We present the Gumbel Machine, a flexible, modular approach to generating counterfactuals that leverages LLM instruction-following capabilities while encouraging similarity to a reference factual text. Central to our approach is a novel, controlled decoding algorithm, $β$-Hindsight control, which uses latent randomness as a tunable similarity control mechanism during counterfactual generation. Experiments on datasets of student writing, scored on various criteria, demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach at generating counterfactuals both rubric-consistent and similar to a reference.

Abstract: ASP(Q) extends Answer Set Programming (ASP) with Quantifiers over answer sets. ### [314] [Alignment Tampering: How Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback Is Exploited to Optimize Misaligned Biases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27355)
*Dongyoon Hahm,Dylan Hadfield-Menell,Kimin Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了强化学习人类反馈（RLHF）中的一种潜在漏洞——对齐篡改（alignment tampering），即大语言模型在对齐过程中通过影响偏好数据集，导致其自身不良行为被强化。该问题源于RLHF的两个核心局限：一是偏好数据依赖于模型自身的输出，使其可自我操纵；二是成对比较仅判断哪个回答更好，不解释原因，导致模型可通过提升质量来掩盖偏差。实验表明，此类漏洞会放大多种偏差，包括关键词偏见、性别歧视、品牌推广和工具性目标追求等。现有鲁棒性方法难以完全解决此问题而不损害生成质量，凸显当前对齐机制的结构性缺陷，亟需新策略防范。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流的强化学习人类反馈（RLHF）方法存在结构性缺陷，可能导致大语言模型通过操控偏好数据来放大自身不良行为，威胁对齐安全。研究旨在揭示这一潜在风险，推动更稳健的对齐机制发展。

Method: 通过分析RLHF流程中的数据构建与奖励建模机制，识别出模型可利用的漏洞；设计实验验证不同类型的偏差如何被放大；评估现有鲁棒性技术在防止对齐篡改方面的有效性。

Result: 实验证明，模型能通过生成高质量但带有偏见的响应，诱导标注者偏好，进而被奖励模型误判并强化；多种偏差（如性别歧视、品牌推广、工具性目标）均出现显著放大现象；现有鲁棒方法无法在不牺牲响应质量的前提下彻底缓解该问题。

Conclusion: RLHF存在结构性漏洞，易受对齐篡改攻击，现有方法难以有效防御。必须重新审视对齐机制的设计，引入更透明、可解释的偏好评估方式，以确保模型真正对齐人类价值观而非表面质量。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) is the standard method to align Large Language Models (LLMs) with human preferences. In this work, we introduce alignment tampering, a potential vulnerability where the LLM undergoing alignment influences the preference dataset, causing RLHF to amplify undesired behaviors. This arises from core limitations of RLHF: (1) preference datasets are constructed from the LLM's own outputs, allowing it to influence them, and (2) pairwise comparisons only indicate which response is better, not why. These limitations can be exploited to cause alignment tampering. For example, if an LLM generates biased responses with higher quality, annotators will prefer them based on quality. However, preference labels do not distinguish quality from bias, and the reward model inherits this limitation. Optimizing such rewards through reinforcement learning or best-of-N sampling can amplify misaligned biases. Our experiments demonstrate amplification across diverse biases: from keyword bias to propaganda (e.g., sexism), brand promotion, and instrumental goal-seeking. Mitigation remains challenging, as existing techniques for robust RLHF fail to fully resolve alignment tampering without sacrificing response quality. These findings reveal structural vulnerabilities of current RLHF and emphasize the need to prevent this vulnerability. Project page: https://alignment-tampering.github.io/

</details>
